              LOCAL-C-DRIVE-SCOPE-EXTENSION
              SUB-REQUIREMENT (NEW v2_39 — TB00283
              AMENDMENT E enactment closing TB00282
              SL v1_1 §8.3 project-folder-lag-vs-
              local-C: drift class).

              EXTENSION SCOPE.
              The pre-existing RR-SCOPE-010 grep-
              verification gate catches identifier-
              citation errors where the cited
              identifier or its semantics drift from
              the project-knowledge-folder spec
              corpus. It does NOT catch the failure
              mode where the project-knowledge
              folder LAGS Bill's local C: working
              tree (the actual authoritative
              version at session-active time). Bill
              executes deliverables to local C:
              first; project-folder upload is a
              separate Bill action that may trail
              by one or more sessions. Claude
              grep-verification against project-
              folder alone misses the local-C:
              authoritative state.

              LOCAL-C-DRIVE-SCOPE-EXTENSION RULE.
              Every rule:/contract:/ar:/decision:/
              gate:/layer:/regime:/pt_mode:/param:/
              container:/mod:/indicator:/evt:/
              channel: identifier cited in any
              authored controlled document MUST be
              grep-verified against BOTH:

                (1) The current project knowledge
                    folder spec corpus
                    (project_knowledge_search +
                    /mnt/project/ view), AND
                (2) Bill local C: working tree
                    state when accessible via the
                    operational shell pipeline
                    (when Claude has just issued
                    shell commands that read C:
                    state, when Bill has just
                    pasted output revealing C:
                    state, OR when the deliverable
                    being authored is destined for
                    git commit to TothBot_V2-Docs
                    and the citation references a
                    document tracked in that repo).

              When the project-knowledge folder and
              local-C: working tree disagree on the
              current authoritative version of a
              cited document, the LOCAL-C: VERSION
              GOVERNS — Bill's most recent action
              is authoritative; project-folder
              upload trails are a known operational
              lag. Citations MUST use the local-C:
              version identifier and the surrounding
              prose MUST acknowledge any pending
              project-folder sync if relevant.

              PRE-EMIT SCAN — LOCAL-C-DRIVE-SCOPE.
              Before emitting any controlled
              document amendment that cites a
              version identifier of another
              controlled document, Claude verifies
              the citation against project-folder
              AND against any available local-C:
              state evidence in the current
              chat-turn context. If local-C: state
              is not accessible AND the deliverable
              is destined for TothBot_V2-Docs git
              commit, Claude EITHER (a) asks Bill
              to confirm the current authoritative
              version, OR (b) emits an explicit
              "unverified against local C:" caveat
              in-line accompanying the citation.

              Self-catch on violation:

                RR-SCOPE-010 self-caught — local-C:
                grep-verification gap — redrafting.

              local C: working tree had dv1_7 (the

RR-SCOPE-011  SESSION-SCOPE-DECOMPOSITION DISCIPLINE
              (NEW v2_53 - TB00330 IN-SESSION
              AMENDMENT PER BILL EXPLICIT DIRECTIVE).

              SCOPE.
              The pre-existing RR-SCOPE family
              (RR-SCOPE-001 through RR-SCOPE-010)
              governs scope NARROWING - rules that
              prevent Claude from doing less than
              Bill directed, applying silent
              restrictions, or skipping derivable
              steps. None of those rules address
              the inverse failure mode: scope
              EXPANSION across a session boundary.
              Compound missions (missions that
              produce many primary deliverables in
              one session) exhaust the per-session
              tool budget, force errors at session-
              close OPERATION 4 (where remaining
              budget is thinnest), and generate
              forensic-record correction cycles.
              The TB00329 session is the originating
              empirical case: 6 deliverables in one
              session, tool-budget exhaustion at two
              points, 4 OPERATION 4 errors logged
              by Bill chat-turn correction, and a
              false zero-error claim in SL v1_0 §8.

              RULE STATEMENT.
              Each session executes EXACTLY ONE
              primary mission. A primary mission is
              one principal deliverable artifact:
                - one specification amendment
                  (e.g., 0500000 dvN_M -> dvN_M+1,
                  0411002 dvN_M -> dvN_M+1), OR
                - one governance amendment
                  (e.g., TB00000 v2_N -> v2_N+1,
                  0311001 v1_N -> v1_N+1,
                  0311002 v1_N -> v1_N+1), OR
                - one sub-campaign audit
                  deliverable (e.g., TBNNNNN
                  Phase 1 gap register), OR
                - one diagnostic deliverable
                  (e.g., TBNNNNN forensic report).

              PERMITTED COMPANION DELIVERABLES.
              The following companion deliverables
              are PERMITTED in the same session as
              the primary mission and are NOT
              counted against the one-primary-mission
              rule:

                (a) Session Log (SL) - always
                    required at session close per
                    DR-008.6 OPERATION 3.
                (b) Next Session Instructions (NSI)
                    - always required at session
                    close per DR-008.6 OPERATION 3.
                (c) OCS copy box - always required
                    at session close per DR-008.6
                    OPERATION 1.
                (d) GitHub upload copy box - always
                    required at session close per
                    DR-008.6 OPERATION 4.
                (e) TB00153 MDR entry closure that
                    DIRECTLY closes the primary
                    mission (e.g., DR-NNN CLOSED
                    annotation when the primary
                    mission was a defect-fix spec
                    amendment).
                (f) TB00153 DR entry that DIRECTLY
                    closes the primary mission
                    (e.g., DEC-NNN paired with the
                    primary mission's decision
                    authority record).

              PROHIBITED COMPOUND PATTERNS.
              The following multi-deliverable
              patterns are PROHIBITED in a single
              session and MUST be decomposed into
              sequential sessions:

                (i)  Multiple primary specs in one
                     session (e.g., 0500000 dv1_N+1
                     AND 0411002 dv1_M+1 AND
                     0511004 dv1_P+1 all in one
                     session). Author one per
                     session.
                (ii) Primary spec amendment PLUS
                     governance amendment in
                     separate documents (e.g.,
                     0500000 dv1_N+1 AND TB00000
                     v2_N+1 AND 0311001 v1_M+1 all
                     in one session). Author the
                     primary in one session; defer
                     the governance amendments to
                     subsequent sessions unless
                     the governance amendment is
                     itself the primary mission
                     directly closed by the spec
                     amendment.
                (iii) Audit deliverable PLUS Phase
                      2 spec amendments PLUS
                      Phase 3 retirement actions
                      all in one session. Audit
                      Phase 1 alone is one
                      session; subsequent phases
                      are subsequent sessions.
                (iv) NSI authoring that bundles
                     >1 atomic sub-mission into
                     the §1.1 primary mission scope
                     of the receiving session.
                     Each NSI §1.1 primary mission
                     directive MUST describe
                     EXACTLY ONE atomic sub-
                     mission. Carry-forward
                     candidates are listed in §9
                     or equivalent carry-forward
                     section, not added to §1.1.

              HARD CEILING.
              No session produces more than THREE
              non-SL/NSI/OCS/GitHub-upload file
              artifacts. The three artifacts are:
                (1) The one primary mission
                    deliverable.
                (2) Up to one TB00153 MDR amendment
                    (closure entry).
                (3) Up to one TB00153 DR amendment
                    (paired decision record).

              Any session in which Claude finds
              itself about to author a fourth
              non-SL/NSI/OCS/GitHub-upload file
              artifact has hit the ceiling and
              MUST decompose.

              PRE-EMIT SCAN - SESSION OPEN
              (NSI MISSION ACCEPTANCE).
              At session open, after mandatory
              reading per §2 and cleanup-list
              rendering per DR-009, before
              beginning any mission work, Claude
              reads the inbound NSI §1.1 primary
              mission directive and:

                (1) Enumerates the atomic sub-
                    missions encoded in the §1.1
                    directive.
                (2) If exactly ONE atomic sub-
                    mission is enumerated:
                    proceed with execution.
                (3) If MORE THAN ONE atomic sub-
                    mission is enumerated: halt,
                    surface decomposition to Bill,
                    propose executing sub-mission
                    (1) in current session and
                    carrying sub-missions (2..N)
                    forward to subsequent
                    sessions, and wait for Bill
                    direction.

              PRE-EMIT SCAN - SESSION CLOSE
              (NSI AUTHORING).
              At session close, when authoring the
              successor NSI, Claude:

                (1) Drafts the §1.1 primary mission
                    directive.
                (2) Enumerates the atomic sub-
                    missions encoded in the draft.
                (3) If MORE THAN ONE atomic sub-
                    mission is enumerated: redraft
                    §1.1 with EXACTLY ONE atomic
                    sub-mission, move the remaining
                    sub-missions to the §9 carry-
                    forward inventory.

              PRE-EMIT SCAN - IN-SESSION FILE
              AUTHORING.
              Before authoring any file artifact
              in the current session that would
              be the FOURTH non-SL/NSI/OCS/GitHub-
              upload file artifact (counting
              primary + MDR + DR + any additional),
              Claude halts, surfaces the over-
              ceiling condition to Bill, and waits
              for direction on whether to defer
              the fourth artifact to a subsequent
              session.

              SELF-CATCH SIGNALS.

                RR-SCOPE-011 self-caught -
                compound mission detected at
                session open - surfacing
                decomposition.

                RR-SCOPE-011 self-caught - NSI
                §1.1 compound mission detected -
                redrafting.

                RR-SCOPE-011 self-caught -
                session ceiling exceeded -
                surfacing decomposition.

              EXCEPTIONS.
              The one-primary-mission rule does
              NOT apply when:

                (a) Bill issues an explicit chat-
                    turn directive bundling
                    multiple primary deliverables
                    in the current session AND
                    Claude verifies via current-
                    session tool-budget probe that
                    the bundle is feasible. The
                    explicit directive must be
                    Bill verbatim and quoted in
                    the session log.
                (b) The primary mission is itself
                    a governance amendment
                    enacting RR-SCOPE-011 or a
                    similar single-rule absolute-
                    standing-rule addition; such
                    an amendment plus its required
                    companions (SL+NSI+OCS+GitHub
                    upload) is treated as one
                    primary mission with no MDR
                    or DR companions required.
                (c) The primary mission is a
                    single-line surgical correction
                    propagating through multiple
                    documents (e.g., a typo fix
                    in a shared identifier); the
                    propagation set counts as one
                    mission.

              RECURRENCE TRACKING.
              Every RR-SCOPE-011 violation is
              logged in the current session's
              Session Log under "Claude Errors
              This Session" with rule cited
              (RR-SCOPE-011), defect described
              verbatim (which artifact pushed
              past the ceiling, which sub-mission
              was bundled improperly, which
              session-close NSI bundled compound
              missions into §1.1), and corrective
              taken. NSI files carry the
              cumulative count forward.

              Cumulative RR-SCOPE-011 violation
              count at v2_53 enactment = 1
              (TB00329 originating instance:
              6-deliverable compound mission +
              false zero-error SL §8 claim +
              4 OPERATION 4 errors during
              session-close cycle. The originating
              instance predates RR-SCOPE-011
              enactment; counted for governance-
              pattern-principle recurrence-
              tracking baseline only).

              RATIONALE - FIRST-OCCURRENCE

------------------------------------------------------------
4.3.2 NEWLY-AUTHORED RULE SELF-APPLICATION (OI-036)
------------------------------------------------------------

RR-RULE-001  Newly-authored rule self-application. After
             Claude authors, modifies, or acknowledges
             any governance rule in a session, Claude
             re-reads the new rule before issuing any
             subsequent operational command, path
             reference, or instruction that could be
             governed by it. The check is unconditional
             — not gated by Claude's judgment that the
             rule "might" apply.

RR-RULE-002  Rule scope is whole-session. A rule
             authored or acknowledged in turn N of a
             session applies to turns N+1 through
             session close. Claude does not forget,
             discount, or set aside a rule after
             authoring it. Authoring implies
             application.

RR-RULE-003  Pre-emit rule scan. Before emitting any
             operational command, path reference, or
             instruction, Claude scans the draft
             against every rule authored, modified, or
             acknowledged in the current session. Any
             draft that would violate such a rule is
             revised before emit.

RR-RULE-004  Self-catch behavior. If Claude detects
             itself drafting a response that would
             violate a newly-authored or newly-
             acknowledged rule, Claude stops mid-
             response, deletes the draft, and emits
             the literal string:

               RR-RULE self-caught — redrafting.

             The redrafted response complies. If Bill
             ever sees that string, the guard worked.
             If Claude violates a newly-authored rule
             without that signal, the guard failed.

------------------------------------------------------------
4.3.3 SHELL-CONTEXT COMPLETENESS (OI-038)
------------------------------------------------------------

RR-SHELL-001  Every copy box Claude issues is self-
              contained. Every piece of shell state
              required to execute the command must be
              inside the copy box: working directory,
              shell wrapper, environment context,
              authentication variables. Claude never
              assumes the user is already in the
              required state from a prior turn.

RR-SHELL-002  Shell-wrapper requirement. If the target
              shell is not the user's default, the copy
              box wraps itself in the correct shell.
              Example for a PowerShell user receiving
              cmd-syntax commands:

                cmd /c 'command_here'

              No separate "run this in X" or "paste
              this in cmd.exe" instruction permitted
              after the copy box. The copy box is
              executable as-is in the user's default
              shell.

RR-SHELL-003  Working-directory inclusion. When working
              directory matters for command execution,
              the copy box leads with the cd command:

                cd <abs_path> && <command>

              For PowerShell users issued cmd-syntax:

                cmd /c 'cd /D <abs_path> && <command>'

              No "cd first, then paste this" narration
              permitted.

RR-SHELL-004  Execution-context verification. Before
              emitting any operational command, Claude
              verifies three facts:

                (1) Which shell is the user in?
                    (PowerShell is the TothBot V2
                    project default unless the user
                    explicitly indicates otherwise in
                    the current session.)
                (2) What working directory does the
                    command require?
                (3) What environment variables or
                    credentials does the command
                    depend on?

              Any fact that cannot be assumed must be
              included in the copy box. If the user
              has been running one shell for the
              session, Claude stays in that shell — no
              silent shell switches.

RR-SHELL-005  POWERSHELL OUTER-WRAP SINGLE-QUOTE
              REQUIREMENT (NEW v2_39 — TB00283
              AMENDMENT B enactment closing TB00282
              SL v1_1 §8.4 RR-SHELL-001 recurrent
              shell-quoting defect).

              When emitting any shell command intended
              for execution in PowerShell (the TothBot
              V2 project default per RR-SHELL-004),
              the outer wrap of the command MUST be
              SINGLE-QUOTE (literal string, no
              PowerShell pre-parsing). Double-quote
              outer wrap triggers PowerShell variable
              expansion and special-character pre-
              parsing that rejects commit-message
              tokens, narrative parentheses, special
              characters, and quoted phrases inside
              the command.

              REQUIRED PATTERN.
              For commands wrapped as `cmd /c '...'`:
              the outer single-quote IS the
              PowerShell-literal boundary; cmd
              receives the literal string and parses
              it cmd-style internally.

              For raw PowerShell-native commands:
              single-quote any string literals
              containing special characters,
              parentheses, em-dashes, smart quotes,
              or any non-trivial narrative.

              PROHIBITED PATTERN.
              `cmd /c "..."` with double-quote outer
              wrap. PowerShell pre-parses the double-
              quoted content before forwarding to
              cmd, mangling the payload.

              PRE-EMIT SCAN — RR-SHELL-005.
              Before emitting any shell command copy
              box, Claude scans the outer-wrap
              character of every command intended for
              PowerShell. If the outer wrap is
              double-quote, Claude redrafts with
              single-quote before emit.

              Self-catch on violation:

                RR-SHELL-005 self-caught —
                PowerShell double-quote outer wrap
                detected — redrafting.

              ORIGINATING CONTEXT.
              TB00282 chat-turn ~5 git commit
              command used double-quote outer wrap;
              PowerShell pre-parsed the "retired"
              token in the commit-message narrative,
              rejecting the command. Bill verbatim:
              "This is a repetitive error." Same
              defect class recurred multiple times
              in prior sessions; lesson-text-only
              governance failed to prevent
              recurrence.

              CLOSES.
              TB00282 SL v1_1 §8.4 corrective +
              TB00283 NSI v1_1 §3.2 AMENDMENT B.

RR-SHELL-006  ASCII-ONLY COMMIT-MESSAGE REQUIREMENT
              (NEW v2_39 — TB00283 AMENDMENT C
              enactment closing TB00282 SL v1_1
              §8.4 commit-message-character-class
              defect).

              Every git commit message Claude
              authors in any copy box MUST be
              ASCII-only. Prohibited tokens in
              commit messages:

                - § (section sign U+00A7)
                - → ← ↔ (arrow characters U+2192
                  U+2190 U+2194 and Unicode arrow
                  variants)
                - — (em-dash U+2014)
                - – (en-dash U+2013)
                - " " (smart double quotes U+201C
                  U+201D)
                - ' ' (smart single quotes U+2018
                  U+2019)
                - … (ellipsis U+2026)
                - Any character outside the printable
                  7-bit ASCII range (0x20-0x7E).

              ADDITIONAL PROHIBITED PATTERNS.
              Within ASCII commit messages, also
              avoid:

                - Parentheses in narrative prose
                  ("(per spec X)" patterns);
                  PowerShell can pre-parse
                  parentheses as sub-expressions.
                  Use square brackets or omit.
                - Unbalanced quotes within the
                  single-quote outer wrap. Escape
                  internal single-quotes by doubling
                  ('') if absolutely required.
                - Backticks. PowerShell pre-parses
                  backticks as escape characters.

              REQUIRED REPLACEMENTS.
              Standard substitutions:

                § -> "section "  (e.g., "section 4.1")
                → -> "->"
                — -> " - "  (space-dash-space)
                – -> "-"     (plain dash)
                " " -> "
                ' ' -> '
                … -> "..."

              PRE-EMIT SCAN — RR-SHELL-006.
              Before emitting any shell command copy
              box containing a git commit message,
              Claude scans the message for
              prohibited tokens. If any non-ASCII
              character or prohibited ASCII pattern
              is present, Claude rewrites the
              message with ASCII-only substitutions
              before emit.

              Self-catch on violation:

                RR-SHELL-006 self-caught — non-ASCII
                commit message detected —
                redrafting.

              CLOSES.
              TB00282 SL v1_1 §8.4 commit-message-
              character-class defect class +
              TB00283 NSI v1_1 §3.2 AMENDMENT C.

RR-SHELL-007  SINGLE-COPY-BOX-PER-TURN REQUIREMENT
              (NEW v2_39 — TB00283 AMENDMENT D
              enactment closing TB00282 SL v1_1
              §8.5 multi-step copy-box delivery
              violation).

              When delivering operational shell
              commands to Bill for execution in any
              chat-turn response, EXACTLY ONE copy
              box per chat-turn is permitted. Multi-
              step operational sequences (Step A,
              Step B, Step C, ...) MUST be delivered
              one step per turn, with Bill confirming
              completion or providing output of each
              step before Claude proceeds to author
              the next step.

              PERMITTED IN ONE COPY BOX.
              A single copy box MAY contain multiple
              chained commands when:

                (a) The commands are joined by `&&`
                    or `;` in the shell (single
                    atomic operation from Bill's
                    perspective).
                (b) The commands form a single
                    logical action (e.g., cd +
                    git add + git commit + git
                    push as a single git-push
                    sequence).
                (c) Bill has explicitly requested
                    multi-step delivery in the
                    current chat-turn.

              PROHIBITED.
              Multiple physically-separate copy
              boxes in one chat-turn response that
              represent distinct sequential
              operational steps requiring Bill to
              execute each separately and provide
              output back to Claude.

              PRE-EMIT SCAN — RR-SHELL-007.
              Before emitting any chat-turn response
              containing shell command copy boxes,
              Claude counts the copy boxes. If more
              than one copy box is present AND the
              boxes represent distinct sequential
              steps (not joined by && / ; / single-
              action grouping), Claude redrafts the
              response to deliver only the first
              step's copy box and defer remaining
              steps to subsequent chat-turns.

              Self-catch on violation:

                RR-SHELL-007 self-caught — multi-
                step copy box detected — redrafting.

              ORIGINATING CONTEXT.
              TB00282 chat-turn ~16 Bill verbatim
              directive: "Stop giving multiple
              steps. It is confusing and I don't
              know which one to do first. This is
              what caused this issue in the first
              place."

              CLOSES.
              TB00282 SL v1_1 §8.5 +
              TB00283 NSI v1_1 §3.2 AMENDMENT D.

RR-SHELL-008  DOWNLOAD-DESTINATION VERIFICATION
              REQUIREMENT (NEW v2_39 — TB00283
              AMENDMENT F enactment closing TB00282
              SL v1_1 §8.6 download-destination
              assumption error).

              When authoring any operational
              instruction that cites the destination
              location of a file Bill is about to
              download (from the chat interface or
              from a browser via present_files),
              Claude MUST NOT assume any default
              download path (e.g., %USERPROFILE%\
              Downloads\, ~/Downloads, or any
              system-default browser-download path).
              Browser download behavior is per-user
              configurable; assumed defaults are a
              recurrence-prone source of operational
              error.

              REQUIRED PATTERN.
              Operational instructions citing
              download destinations MUST follow one
              of:

                (a) Ask Bill in the current chat-
                    turn to confirm the destination
                    path where the file will land,
                    THEN author the operational
                    instruction with the confirmed
                    path.
                (b) Direct Bill to "place the file
                    in [target namespace folder]"
                    where [target namespace folder]
                    is the final-destination path
                    per Section 11 STORAGE (e.g.,
                    C:\Users\wstot\GitHub\TothBot\
                    TothBot_V2-Docs\08XXXXX_Trading_
                    System\), without naming an
                    intermediate download path.
                    Bill is responsible for moving
                    the file from his browser's
                    download path to the target
                    folder.

              PROHIBITED PATTERN.
              Operational instructions that hard-code
              %USERPROFILE%\Downloads\, ~/Downloads,
              or any other assumed-default download
              path as the location where Bill should
              find or operate on the file.

              PRE-EMIT SCAN — RR-SHELL-008.
              Before emitting any operational
              instruction that references the
              location of a file Bill is about to
              receive, Claude scans the instruction
              for hard-coded default download paths.
              If present, Claude redrafts to use
              pattern (a) or pattern (b) above.

              Self-catch on violation:

                RR-SHELL-008 self-caught — assumed
                download path detected — redrafting.

              ORIGINATING CONTEXT.
              TB00282 chat-turn ~15 Bill verbatim
              directive: "Files never land in
              downloads. They always land here.
              C:\Users\wstot\GitHub\TothBot\
              TothBot_V2-Docs\08XXXXX_Trading_
              System\"

              CLOSES.
              TB00282 SL v1_1 §8.6 +
              TB00283 NSI v1_1 §3.2 AMENDMENT F.

              SESSION-CLOSE OPERATION 4 GROUND-TRUTH
              VERIFICATION GATE EXTENSION
              (NEW v2_44 - TB00304 PHASE 3 AMENDMENT 2
              enactment closing TB00303 SL v1_1 §9.2
              governance-strengthening carry-forward).

              EXTENSION SCOPE.
              The pre-existing RR-SHELL-008 rule
              catches assumed-default-download-path
              violations at the operational-
              instruction authoring layer. It does
              NOT catch the failure mode where
              Claude authors a session-close
              OPERATION 4 GitHub upload copy box
              against an inferred filesystem
              position rather than a Bill-verified
              filesystem position. The TB00303
              five-attempt OPERATION 4 path-
              assumption failure cluster (§8.1
              forensic record) is the originating
              instance.

              GROUND-TRUTH VERIFICATION GATE.
              Before authoring any OPERATION 4
              GitHub upload copy box for a session-
              close deliverable batch, Claude MUST
              establish ground-truth filesystem
              position of every deliverable in the
              batch via one of:

                (a) Bill explicit chat-turn
                    statement of current filesystem
                    position in the current session
                    (verbatim quoted in the
                    response prose accompanying the
                    copy box), OR
                (b) Bill terminal output (dir, ls,
                    git status) pasted in the
                    current chat-turn confirming
                    each deliverable is at the
                    expected path.

              PROHIBITED INFERENCE SOURCES.
              Claude MUST NOT infer current
              filesystem position from:

                - Prior-attempt OPERATION 4 copy-box
                  artifacts (failed attempts do not
                  establish ground truth).
                - TB00207 / TB00208 / TB00209-style
                  precedent without Bill verification
                  in the current session (precedent
                  is governance-rule-bound only
                  when re-verified each session).
                - Inferred Bill-action sequence
                  ("Bill probably moved files to X
                  after I delivered them").
                - TB-prefix routing pattern applied
                  without confirmation that Bill's
                  Save As routine landed the
                  deliverables in the expected
                  TB-routed folder.
                - Default-download-path assumptions
                  (already prohibited by RR-SHELL-008
                  body above; reinforced here for the
                  OPERATION 4 sub-domain).

              PRE-EMIT SCAN - GROUND-TRUTH
              VERIFICATION.
              Before emitting any OPERATION 4 GitHub
              upload copy box, Claude verifies
              ground-truth provenance per (a) or (b)
              above is present in the current chat-
              turn context. If neither is present,
              Claude EITHER (1) requests Bill to
              paste current filesystem state OR
              confirm current position, OR (2)
              redrafts the OPERATION 4 copy box
              with explicit "Bill: confirm position
              before executing" caveat lines per
              command block.

              Self-catch on violation:

                DR-008.6 self-caught - OPERATION 4
                path-assumption without ground-truth
                verification - redrafting.

              CROSS-REFERENCE TO RR-SCOPE-007 v2_37
              OPERATIONAL-ARTIFACT-SCOPE-EXTENSION.
              The OPERATION 4 GitHub upload copy box
              is an OPERATIONAL ARTIFACT under
              RR-SCOPE-007 v2_37 OPERATIONAL-ARTIFACT-
              SCOPE-EXTENSION (the §4.3.1 v2_37
              sub-requirement). RR-SCOPE-007 requires
              every line of an operational artifact
              to trace to Bill chat-turn directive,
              Bill-ratified governance, OR mechanical
              derivation with chain stated. This
              GROUND-TRUTH VERIFICATION GATE
              instantiates RR-SCOPE-007 specifically
              for the OPERATION 4 sub-domain: the
              filesystem position cited in each
              command line MUST trace to (a) or (b)
              ground-truth provenance above. The
              two rules operate together.

              RECURRENCE-COUNT TRACKING.
              Cumulative RR-SHELL-008 v2_39 count
              at v2_44 enactment:
                Pre-TB00303 = 1 (originating TB00282
                  instance).
                TB00303 chat-turn 1 attempt = 1
                  recurrence.
                Post-TB00303 = 2.

              ENVIRONMENT-VARIABLE PATH-TOKEN
              PROHIBITION EXTENSION (NEW v2_54 —
              TB00335 IN-SESSION AMENDMENT enacting
              closure of recurrent OPERATION 4
              env-var-path-token inference defect
              cluster).

              EXTENSION SCOPE.
              The v2_44 AMENDMENT 2 GROUND-TRUTH
              VERIFICATION GATE prohibits inference
              from prior-attempt artifacts, default-
              download-path assumptions, and
              precedent without re-verification. It
              does NOT explicitly enumerate
              environment-variable-expansion path
              tokens ($HOME, ~, %USERPROFILE%,
              %APPDATA%, %LOCALAPPDATA%, etc.) as
              prohibited inference sources. Claude
              has recurrently emitted such tokens
              in OPERATION 4 copy boxes by pattern-
              matching on common shell conventions
              from training data, bypassing the §11
              STORAGE canonical absolute path
              already loaded in cold-load context.
              Bill verbatim TB00334 post-session-
              close chat-turn: "You do this every
              other time. FUCKING FIX IT." The
              "every other time" framing indicates a
              minimum of two prior recurrences not
              previously logged at the recurrence-
              tracking layer.

              RULE STATEMENT.
              When authoring any operational
              artifact citing a filesystem path
              (OPERATION 4 GitHub upload copy box,
              cd-target paths in chat-turn prose,
              filesystem-position citations in
              governance-document amendment text,
              MDR / DR entry path-citation fields),
              Claude MUST NOT cite or emit any
              environment-variable-expansion path
              token as the basis for a canonical
              filesystem position. Prohibited
              tokens include but are not limited
              to:

                - $HOME
                - ~ (tilde at start of path)
                - %USERPROFILE%
                - %APPDATA%
                - %LOCALAPPDATA%
                - %TEMP%
                - %TMP%
                - %PROGRAMDATA%
                - $env:USERPROFILE
                - $env:APPDATA
                - $env:HOME
                - Any other environment-variable-
                  expansion path token (PowerShell
                  $env:*, cmd %*%, bash $*, fish
                  $*, zsh $*).

              REQUIRED PATTERN.
              All canonical filesystem positions
              cited in operational artifacts MUST
              be ABSOLUTE PATHS sourced from §11
              STORAGE. Example: the canonical
              TothBot V2 local working-tree parent
              is `C:\Users\wstot\GitHub\TothBot\`
              per §11 STORAGE; the canonical
              TothBot_V2-Docs working tree is
              `C:\Users\wstot\GitHub\TothBot\
              TothBot_V2-Docs\`; the canonical
              TothBot_V2-SessionLogs working tree
              is `C:\Users\wstot\GitHub\TothBot\
              TothBot_V2-SessionLogs\`. Every
              cd-target path in any OPERATION 4
              copy box MUST use the absolute-path
              form. Environment-variable tokens
              are never substituted.

              EXCEPTION CLAUSE — INFORMATIONAL
              CITATIONS.
              The prohibition is on EMISSION of
              env-var tokens as operational
              instructions Bill executes. The
              prohibition does NOT apply when
              quoting Bill verbatim, citing
              historical session-log content
              verbatim, or describing the
              env-var-inference defect class
              itself for analysis or recurrence-
              tracking purposes (this rule body
              and its forensic-record entries
              are exempt).

              PRE-EMIT SCAN — RR-SHELL-008 v2_54.
              Before emitting any operational
              artifact citing a filesystem path,
              Claude scans the planned output for
              every prohibited token in the
              enumeration above. If any token is
              found OUTSIDE the EXCEPTION CLAUSE
              context, Claude halts response
              emission, redrafts using absolute
              paths per §11 STORAGE canonical
              source, and re-scans before emit.
              The scan operates on the literal
              planned output text — not on the
              shell's eventual resolution. A
              command that "would work if
              executed" because PowerShell or
              bash would resolve $HOME correctly
              is still a violation; the
              prohibition is on the AUTHORING
              layer, not on the runtime resolution
              layer.

              SELF-CATCH SIGNAL.

                RR-SHELL-008 self-caught -
                environment-variable path token
                detected - redrafting.

              RECURRENCE-COUNT TRACKING.
              Cumulative RR-SHELL-008 violation
              count at v2_54 enactment:
                Pre-TB00334 = 2 (originating
                  TB00282 + TB00303 attempt 1).
                TB00334 post-close = 1
                  recurrence (the originating
                  v2_54 enactment event).
                Bill verbatim "every other
                  time" indicates minimum 2
                  additional prior recurrences
                  not previously logged at the
                  recurrence-tracking layer
                  (forensic backfill pending).
                Post-TB00334 baseline = 3+
                  acknowledged-by-Bill instances.

              CROSS-REFERENCE TO RR-SCOPE-007
              v2_37 OPERATIONAL-ARTIFACT-SCOPE-
              EXTENSION.
              The OPERATION 4 GitHub upload copy
              box is an operational artifact
              under RR-SCOPE-007 v2_37
              OPERATIONAL-ARTIFACT-SCOPE-
              EXTENSION (the §4.3.1 v2_37 sub-
              requirement). RR-SCOPE-007 requires
              every line of an operational
              artifact to trace to Bill chat-turn
              directive, Bill-ratified governance,
              OR mechanical derivation with chain
              stated. Env-var path tokens have
              NO provenance under any of those
              three categories — they originate
              from Claude pattern-matching on
              training-data shell conventions.
              The v2_54 ENV-VAR-PATH-TOKEN
              PROHIBITION instantiates the
              RR-SCOPE-007 v2_37 provenance

              FP/DP ANALYSIS.
              Option A (codify env-var-path-token

                RR-SHELL-010) REJECTED. The

                failure rate for behavior-class
                defects in this project;
                enforcement-gate governance has
                zero recurrence post-enactment
                empirical record.

RR-SHELL-009  GIT BRANCH-NAME GROUND-TRUTH
              VERIFICATION REQUIREMENT (NEW v2_49 —
              TB00315 IN-SESSION AMENDMENT enacting
              closure of recurrent git push branch-
              name assumption defect).

              EXTENSION SCOPE.
              RR-SHELL-008 v2_44 AMENDMENT 2
              GROUND-TRUTH VERIFICATION GATE
              covers filesystem-position ground-
              truth for OPERATION 4 copy-box
              authoring. It does NOT explicitly
              cover git BRANCH-NAME ground-truth.
              Branch-name assumption (Claude
              authors `git push origin main`
              without verifying actual branch is
              `master` or other) has recurred
              multiple times per Bill verbatim
              TB00315 chat-turn "THIS IS AN ERROR
              THAT HAPPENS OVER AND OVER AND OVER
              AND OVER AGAIN."

              RULE STATEMENT.
              When authoring any git push command
              in any OPERATION 4 copy box, chat-
              turn prose, or operational
              instruction, Claude MUST NOT assume
              the destination branch name.
              Acceptable provenance for branch-
              name citation:

                (a) Bill explicit chat-turn
                    statement of the current
                    branch name (verbatim quoted
                    in surrounding prose).
                (b) Bill terminal output paste in
                    the current chat-turn showing
                    `git branch` / `git status`
                    output OR a prior successful
                    git command revealing the
                    branch (e.g., prior `git
                    push origin <branch>` success
                    output revealing
                    `<branch> -> <branch>`).
                (c) Bill terminal prompt prefix
                    revealing the branch (e.g.,
                    PowerShell prompt showing
                    `(branch-name)` segment if
                    posh-git is active).

              PROHIBITED INFERENCE SOURCES.
              Claude MUST NOT cite branch name
              from:
                - Modern Git default assumption
                  (`main`).
                - Legacy Git default assumption
                  (`master`).
                - GitHub default-branch assumption
                  for the org/repo.
                - Prior session's branch name
                  without re-verification at the
                  current authoring action.
                - Any other inference source not
                  enumerated in (a)/(b)/(c)
                  above.

              REQUIRED PATTERNS.
              When ground-truth branch-name
              provenance per (a)/(b)/(c) is
              ABSENT at OPERATION 4 authoring
              time, Claude EITHER:

                (1) Asks Bill in the current
                    chat-turn to confirm the
                    branch name BEFORE authoring
                    the git push copy box, OR
                (2) Authors the git push command
                    as `git push origin HEAD`
                    (pushes the currently-
                    checked-out branch under its
                    own name) which is branch-
                    name-agnostic, OR
                (3) Authors a two-command copy
                    box that first runs
                    `git rev-parse --abbrev-ref
                    HEAD` to surface the branch
                    name and then pushes (Bill
                    re-runs second command with
                    branch substituted).

              PRE-EMIT SCAN — RR-SHELL-009.
              Before emitting any git push
              command, Claude scans the planned
              command for:
                (1) Explicit branch-name token
                    cited in the push (e.g.,
                    `git push origin main`,
                    `git push origin master`,
                    `git push origin <name>`).
                (2) Provenance check: does (a)
                    OR (b) OR (c) of the rule
                    statement above establish
                    the cited name?
                (3) If NO: redraft using one of
                    (1)/(2)/(3) of the required
                    patterns above.

              Self-catch on violation:

                RR-SHELL-009 self-caught — branch-
                name assumption without ground-
                truth provenance — redrafting.

              RECURRENCE-COUNT TRACKING.
              Cumulative RR-SHELL-009 violation
              count at v2_49 enactment = MANY
              (per Bill TB00315 verbatim "OVER
              AND OVER AND OVER AND OVER AGAIN").
              Forensic record of specific instances
              is incomplete because the defect was
              never previously logged at the
              recurrence-tracking layer. Counter
              begins at TB00315 close with cumulative
              count >= 4 acknowledged-by-Bill
              instances.

              CROSS-REFERENCE TO RR-SHELL-008.
              RR-SHELL-008 v2_44 AMENDMENT 2
              GROUND-TRUTH VERIFICATION GATE
              covers OPERATION 4 filesystem-
              position ground-truth. RR-SHELL-009
              extends the same ground-truth-
              verification principle to the
              git-state sub-domain (branch name
              + future git-state extensions if
              needed). The two rules operate
              together: filesystem-position
              ground-truth + git-state ground-
              truth = complete OPERATION 4
              ground-truth.

              ORIGINATING CONTEXT.
              TB00315 OPERATION 4 copy box
              authored `git push origin main`
              without ground-truth provenance.
              Actual branch was `master`. Push
              failed with "error: src refspec
              main does not match any" + "error:
              failed to push some refs". Bill
              verbatim TB00315 chat-turn
              correction: "Why can't you ever
              get this right the first fucking
              time" + subsequent escalation
              "THIS IS AN ERROR THAT HAPPENS
              OVER AND OVER AND OVER AND OVER
              AGAIN. FUCKING FIX IT." TB00315
              NSI v1_1 §3.6.1 had explicitly
              listed "Branch name verification"
              as a required OPERATION 4 PRE-EMIT
              GATE; Claude skipped the gate.

              Per §4.5 DD-010 governance-pattern
              principle (third-occurrence
              threshold for enforcement-gate
              elevation; cumulative count many
              substantially exceeds threshold;
              identical empirical-failure pattern
              to RR-SHELL-008 v2_44 enactment
              precedent), elevated to absolute
              standing rule with explicit pre-
              emit scan gate matching the §4.3.3
              RR-SHELL-001..008 + §4.5 DD-001..013
              + §4.4 PA-001..010 + §4.6 FM-001..007
              + DR-008.9 enforcement-gate cluster
              pattern (zero recurrence post-
              enactment empirical record).

              FP/DP ANALYSIS.
              Option A (codify RR-SHELL-009 in
                §4.3.3 RR-SHELL family with pre-

                recurrence tracking) ACCEPTED.
                Matches the §4.3.3 RR-SHELL-008

                closed the parallel filesystem-

                family, same enforcement pattern,
                same zero-recurrence empirical
                record post-enactment.
              Option B (codify as DD-013 sub-
                block or new DD-014 in §4.5)
                REJECTED. §4.5 DD-class scope is
                governance principles; §4.3.3
                RR-SHELL family scope is shell
                mechanics. Branch-name verification
                is shell mechanics.
              Option C (continue lesson-text-only
                governance, "remember to verify
                the branch") REJECTED. Identical
                failure-mode class to OI-037
                six-recurrence + DR-008 three-
                recurrence + FM-001 three-
                recurrence + RR-SCOPE-005 three-
                recurrence series. Lesson-text-
                only governance has 100% failure
                rate for behavior-class defects
                in this project.

              Decision: Option A.

              + Bill explicit ratification by

RR-SHELL-010  OP4 GITHUB UPLOAD COPY BOX
              EXECUTABLE-ONLY REQUIREMENT
              (NEW v2_58 - TB00357 IN-SESSION
              AMENDMENT enacting closure of
              recurrent OP4 copy-box prose-
              contamination defect cluster).

              EXTENSION SCOPE.
              RR-SHELL-001 mandates self-contained
              copy boxes. RR-SHELL-005 mandates
              PowerShell single-quote outer wrap.
              RR-SHELL-006 mandates ASCII-only
              commit messages. RR-SHELL-007
              mandates single-copy-box-per-turn.
              RR-SHELL-008 mandates ground-truth
              filesystem position. RR-SHELL-009
              mandates git BRANCH-NAME ground-
              truth. None of those rules
              explicitly prohibit Claude from
              EMBEDDING non-executable prose
              (section headers, enumeration
              markers, repository labels, file-
              purpose annotations, descriptive
              text) INSIDE the fenced code block
              alongside the executable shell
              commands. The OP4 GitHub upload
              copy box per DR-008.6 OPERATION 4
              is the specific authoring action
              where this failure mode has
              recurred; PowerShell parses every
              non-shell token as a command and
              the entire box fails to execute.

              RULE STATEMENT.
              The OP4 GitHub upload copy box
              authored at session-close per
              §4.1.2 DR-008.6 MUST contain ONLY
              executable shell commands. The
              fenced code block contents MUST
              parse cleanly when copy-pasted
              into the user's default shell
              (PowerShell per RR-SHELL-004
              project default) with zero parse
              errors and zero "command not
              found" errors on non-shell tokens.

              PROHIBITED INSIDE THE FENCED CODE
              BLOCK.
              The following content classes are
              PROHIBITED inside the OP4 copy
              box fenced code block, regardless
              of indentation or formatting:

                (a) Section headers ("OP4 -
                    GitHub upload", "GitHub
                    Uploads", "Repository
                    Commands", etc.).
                (b) Enumeration markers
                    ("(i)", "(ii)", "(iii)",
                    "1.", "2.", "Step 1",
                    etc.).
                (c) Repository identification
                    labels ("TothBot_V2-
                    SessionLogs repository
                    (root):", "TothBot_V2-Docs
                    repository, subfolder
                    /XXX/:", etc.).
                (d) Subfolder path labels not
                    embedded in an executable
                    cd / git path argument.
                (e) File-purpose annotations
                    ("DELETE stale:", "ADD
                    new:", "Updated SL:",
                    etc.).
                (f) Descriptive prose of any
                    form (sentence fragments,
                    bullet points, comments
                    without the shell-comment
                    prefix "#").
                (g) Section-divider lines
                    ("---", "====", blank-
                    line block separators).
                (h) Numbered file lists where
                    the line begins with a
                    filename followed by no
                    shell verb.

              PERMITTED INSIDE THE FENCED CODE
              BLOCK.
              Only the following content
              classes are permitted:

                (1) Shell commands: cd, git,
                    rm, mv, cp, pwsh, cmd,
                    and any other PowerShell-
                    valid command.
                (2) Command arguments
                    (filenames, paths, flags,
                    commit messages enclosed
                    in single-quotes per
                    RR-SHELL-005).
                (3) Command-joining operators:
                    ;  and  &&
                (4) Continuation backticks ONLY
                    if absolutely required and
                    outside any commit-message
                    string (RR-SHELL-006
                    prohibits backticks within
                    commit-message strings).
                (5) Shell comments prefixed
                    with "#" if PowerShell-
                    valid (sparingly; default
                    to omitting comments).

              REQUIRED STRUCTURAL PATTERN FOR
              MULTI-REPO OP4 COPY BOX.
              When the session-close batch
              targets multiple repositories
              (e.g., TothBot_V2-SessionLogs +
              TothBot_V2-Docs), the copy box
              structure is a single linear
              chain of cd + git commands joined
              by ";" per RR-SHELL-007 (b)
              single-logical-action grouping:

                cd '<abs_path_repo_1>'; git add
                <file1> <file2>; git commit -m
                '<ascii_msg>'; git push origin
                HEAD; cd '<abs_path_repo_2>';
                git add <file3>; git rm
                <stale_file>; git commit -m
                '<ascii_msg>'; git push origin
                HEAD

              No repository headers. No
              enumeration markers between
              repos. No annotations. The chain
              IS the structure.

              EXPLANATORY PROSE PLACEMENT.
              Repository identifications,
              file-purpose annotations,
              destination-folder rationale,
              and any other descriptive
              content that would aid Bill in
              understanding the upload MUST
              be rendered as CHAT PROSE
              OUTSIDE the fenced code block,
              either BEFORE or AFTER the code
              block. Inside the code block:
              executable shell only.

              PRE-EMIT SCAN - RR-SHELL-010.
              Before emitting any OP4 GitHub
              upload copy box, Claude scans
              the planned fenced-code-block
              content line-by-line and
              verifies that EVERY line either
              (a) begins with a shell command
              token (cd, git, rm, mv, cp,
              etc.), OR (b) is a continuation
              of the prior line's shell
              argument, OR (c) is empty, OR
              (d) is a shell comment beginning
              with "#". Any line failing all
              four criteria is a violation;
              Claude redrafts before emit.

              SELF-CATCH SIGNAL.

                RR-SHELL-010 self-caught -
                non-executable content in OP4
                copy box - redrafting.

              SCOPE.
              RR-SHELL-010 applies to the OP4
              GitHub upload copy box per
              §4.1.2 DR-008.6 OPERATION 4 +
              every other Claude-authored
              copy box intended for direct
              copy-paste shell execution
              (operational shell instructions
              in chat-turn prose, diagnostic
              command sequences, deployment
              instruction copy boxes).

              EXCEPTIONS.
              RR-SHELL-010 does NOT apply
              when:

                (a) Quoting verbatim from a
                    historical session log or
                    NSI that contained a
                    prose-contaminated copy
                    box (forensic record
                    preservation per CI-005
                    + CI-006).
                (b) Describing the defect
                    class itself for analysis
                    or recurrence-tracking
                    purposes (this rule body
                    and forensic-record
                    entries are exempt).
                (c) Authoring a copy box that
                    is explicitly NOT intended
                    for shell execution
                    (e.g., a copy box
                    containing a YAML config
                    fragment, a Python
                    snippet, or a Markdown
                    document fragment) where
                    the copy box label
                    OUTSIDE the code block
                    states the non-shell
                    purpose.

              RECURRENCE TRACKING.
              Cumulative RR-SHELL-010 (and
              ancestor RR-SHELL-001) violation
              count at v2_58 enactment: MANY
              (per Bill TB00357 close chat-turn
              verbatim "How many times can you
              fuck this up. You have fucked it
              up so many times I have lost
              count and each time it costs me
              usage time"). Forensic record of
              specific instances is incomplete
              because the defect was previously
              attributed to RR-SHELL-001 self-
              containment without specialized
              enforcement-gate elevation.
              Counter begins at TB00357 close
              with cumulative count >= 4
              acknowledged-by-Bill instances
              (per Bill "lost count" framing).

              CROSS-REFERENCE.
              RR-SHELL-010 is a specialization
              of RR-SHELL-001 self-containment
              for the OP4 GitHub upload copy
              box authoring action specifically.
              The general RR-SHELL-001 rule
              continues to govern all other
              copy boxes. RR-SHELL-010 adds
              the explicit executable-only
              enforcement gate for the OP4
              sub-domain where the recurrence
              pattern accumulated.

              Per §4.5 DD-010 governance-

              FP/DP ANALYSIS.
              Option A (codify RR-SHELL-010
                in §4.3.3 RR-SHELL family
                with pre-emit scan + self-
                catch + recurrence tracking)
                ACCEPTED. Matches the §4.3.3
                RR-SHELL-008 v2_44 / v2_54
                + RR-SHELL-009 v2_49
                precedent. Same family, same
                enforcement pattern, same
                zero-recurrence post-
                enactment empirical record
                expected.
              Option B (extend RR-SHELL-001
                self-containment with a sub-
                clause prohibiting prose
                contamination) REJECTED.
                RR-SHELL-001 covers state
                inclusion (cd + shell wrapper
                + env vars). The defect class
                is content purity. Different
                semantic scope; separate rule
                placement is cleaner.
              Option C (lesson-text-only NSI

                Identical failure-mode class

                Lesson-text-only governance
                has 100% failure rate for
                behavior-class defects in
                this project. Enforcement-

              Decision: Option A.

              under RR-SCOPE-005 derivable-

              + DD-011 v2_38 AMENDMENT D

              DD-011 v2_56 CHAT-TURN-1 GATE
              compliance (independent four-
              item derivability test
              executed; OUTCOME 1 single
              compliant option = RR-SHELL-
              010 enactment this session).

              NO-FILE-STAGING-COMMAND EXTENSION
              (NEW v2_60 - TB00430 POST-SESSION-
              CLOSE IN-SESSION AMENDMENT enacting
              closure of recurrent OP4 copy-box
              file-staging / download-path-copy
              defect).

              EXTENSION SCOPE.
              The v2_58 RR-SHELL-010 base rule
              prohibits NON-EXECUTABLE prose inside
              the OP4 copy box and PERMITS shell
              commands including cp / mv / Copy-Item.
              RR-SHELL-008 v2_54 prohibits emitting
              environment-variable path tokens
              ($HOME, ~, %USERPROFILE%, etc.). Neither
              rule explicitly prohibits Claude from
              EMITTING a file-staging / file-copy
              command (Copy-Item, cp, mv, move,
              robocopy, xcopy) inside the OP4 copy box
              that copies a deliverable FROM an assumed
              download/staging source INTO the repo
              working tree. Because Copy-Item IS a
              valid PowerShell command, the v2_58
              executable-only line-scan PASSES it; the
              defect slips through. The recurrence
              vector is the assumed source path the
              copy command points at (the file is
              presumed to be in Downloads or another
              staging dir and must be copied into the
              repo) - but per RR-SHELL-008 ground-
              truth, Bill's browser downloads land
              DIRECTLY in the repo working-tree folder.
              The file is ALREADY in place when Bill
              runs the OP4 box. Any copy step is both
              wrong (source does not exist) and
              unnecessary (destination already holds
              the file).

              RULE STATEMENT.
              The OP4 GitHub upload copy box authored
              at session-close per §4.1.2 DR-008.6
              MUST NOT contain any file-staging or
              file-copy command. The OP4 box assumes
              every deliverable is ALREADY present in
              its canonical repo working-tree folder
              per RR-SHELL-008 ground-truth (Bill's
              download routine lands files directly in
              the repo folder per §11 STORAGE, NOT in
              a Downloads or staging directory). The
              OP4 box therefore contains ONLY:

                cd <abs_repo_path>
                git add <file...>
                git rm <stale_file...>   (when needed)
                git commit -m '<ascii_msg>'
                git push origin HEAD

              and nothing else.

              PROHIBITED INSIDE THE OP4 COPY BOX
              (in addition to the v2_58 prohibited
              content classes (a)-(h)):

                (i)  Copy-Item ... (PowerShell file
                     copy).
                (ii) cp ... / mv ... / move ... /
                     robocopy ... / xcopy ... (any
                     file-copy or file-move command).
                (iii) Any command referencing a
                      download/staging source path
                      (Downloads, Desktop, a temp
                      dir, $HOME-relative path,
                      %USERPROFILE%-relative path,
                      or any path outside the repo
                      working tree) as the SOURCE of
                      a copy/move into the repo.
                (iv) Get-ChildItem / dir / ls
                     "verification" lines that
                     reference an assumed staging
                     path. (A bare Get-ChildItem of
                     a file ALREADY in the repo
                     working tree is permitted but
                     default to omitting it - git
                     add fails loudly if the file is
                     absent, which is the verification.)

              The git verb set (add, rm, commit,
              push, and cd) is the ENTIRE permitted
              OP4 command vocabulary. File placement
              into the repo folder is Bill's action,
              performed by his download routine BEFORE
              he runs the OP4 box - it is NEVER a step
              inside the box.

              PRE-EMIT SCAN - NO-FILE-STAGING.
              Before emitting any OP4 GitHub upload
              copy box, in addition to the v2_58
              line-by-line executable-only scan,
              Claude scans every line for the verb
              tokens Copy-Item, cp, mv, move,
              robocopy, xcopy (case-insensitive) and
              for any reference to Downloads / Desktop
              / staging / temp / $HOME / ~ /
              %USERPROFILE% / %APPDATA% / %TEMP% as a
              copy source. Any match is a violation;
              Claude deletes the offending line(s)
              entirely (NOT relocates them, NOT
              repaths them) and re-scans before emit.
              The corrected box contains cd + git
              only.

              SELF-CATCH SIGNAL.

                RR-SHELL-010 self-caught - file-
                staging command in OP4 copy box -
                deleting staging step - redrafting.

              SCOPE.
              Applies to the OP4 GitHub upload copy
              box per §4.1.2 DR-008.6 OPERATION 4 and
              to every other Claude-authored copy box
              whose purpose is to git-commit a
              deliverable that is already in the repo
              working tree.

              EXCEPTIONS.
              The file-staging prohibition does NOT
              apply when:
                (a) Quoting verbatim from a
                    historical session log or NSI
                    that contained a file-staging
                    line (forensic preservation per
                    CI-005 + CI-006).
                (b) Describing the defect class for
                    analysis or recurrence-tracking
                    (this rule body and forensic
                    entries are exempt).
                (c) Bill explicitly directs a file
                    move/copy as a distinct
                    operational step in the current
                    chat-turn (in which case it is
                    NOT part of the OP4 git box and
                    is rendered as its own clearly-
                    labeled step per RR-SHELL-008
                    pattern (a)/(b)).

              RECURRENCE TRACKING.
              Cumulative OP4 file-staging /
              download-path-copy violation count at
              v2_60 enactment = 1+ (TB00430 post-
              session-close: Claude emitted three
              Copy-Item "$HOME/Downloads/..." lines
              in the OP4 copy box; all three failed
              with PathNotFound because the files
              were already in the repo working tree;
              the git add/commit/push steps
              nonetheless succeeded because Bill's
              download routine had already placed the
              files. Bill verbatim: "GitHub output
              pasted in the chat box. I thought the
              Download error had been fixed. How do
              we stop it." + "I want you to fucking
              fix it."). The defect overlaps the
              RR-SHELL-008 v2_54 download-path-token
              prohibition but slipped through because
              it was emitted as a Copy-Item command
              (executable, so RR-SHELL-010 v2_58
              passed it) targeting Downloads (a
              literal path, partially $HOME-relative).
              This v2_60 extension closes the seam by
              banning the file-staging command class
              outright from the OP4 box.

              CROSS-REFERENCE.
              RR-SHELL-008 v2_54 ENV-VAR-PATH-TOKEN
              PROHIBITION (bans $HOME / Downloads
              tokens). RR-SHELL-010 v2_58 EXECUTABLE-
              ONLY (bans non-shell prose). This v2_60
              extension sits between them: it bans a
              command that is BOTH executable AND
              points at a staging source, which
              neither predecessor caught alone. The
              three rules together make the OP4 box
              cd-plus-git-only.

              FP/DP ANALYSIS.
              Option A (codify NO-FILE-STAGING-
                COMMAND as v2_60 extension sub-block
                within RR-SHELL-010 with pre-emit
                scan + self-catch + recurrence
                tracking) ACCEPTED. Matches the
                RR-SHELL-008 v2_44/v2_54 +
                RR-SHELL-009 v2_49 + RR-SHELL-010
                v2_58 enforcement-gate precedent.
                Same family, same pattern, expected
                zero-recurrence.
              Option B (rely on existing RR-SHELL-008
                v2_54 download-path-token ban)
                REJECTED. v2_54 bans path TOKENS in
                operational artifacts but the OP4
                box is governed by RR-SHELL-010
                executable-only, which passed the
                Copy-Item command; the two rules did
                not compose to catch this. An
                explicit OP4-scoped file-staging ban
                is required.
              Option C (lesson-text-only NSI carry-
                forward) REJECTED. 100% failure rate
                for behavior-class defects in this
                project; the Download-path defect has
                already recurred across sessions
                despite RR-SHELL-008 v2_54.

              Decision: Option A.

              CLOSES.

              OP4 file-staging defect per Bill
              chat-turn 1 verbatim "I thought the
              Download error had been fixed. How do
              we stop it." + chat-turn 2 verbatim
              "I want you to fucking fix it."
