------------------------------------------------------------
4.3.4 VIOLATION HANDLING
------------------------------------------------------------

RR-VIOL-001  Any Claude response violating any
             RR-SCOPE, RR-RULE, or RR-SHELL rule
             (outside the context of stating or citing
             the rule itself, or executing a self-catch
             per RR-SCOPE-006 / RR-RULE-004) is a
             session-halting defect. Bill's corrective
             is to paste the violation back with the
             originating OI reference (e.g., "OI-037
             recurrence — regenerate") and Claude
             produces a corrected response that
             complies.

RR-VIOL-002  Recurrence tracking. Every RR-* rule
             violation is logged in the current
             session's Session Log under a "Claude
             Errors This Session" section, with rule
             cited, defect described verbatim, and
             corrective taken. NSI files carry the
             recurrence count forward.

------------------------------------------------------------
4.3.5 RATIONALE
------------------------------------------------------------

RR-RAT-001   OI-037 (instruction-following) accumulated
             SIX consecutive session recurrences
             (TB00114 / TB00115 / TB00116 / TB00117 /
             TB00118 / TB00119) under governance-via-
             lesson-text alone. OI-036 and OI-038
             followed the same pattern at lower
             severity. Governance-via-lesson-text has
             demonstrably failed. Absolute standing
             rules with pre-emit scans and self-catch
             signals (matching the Section 4.2 pattern
             that succeeded for the §4.2 ABSOLUTE
             STANDING RULE) are the required
             escalation.

RR-RAT-002   Section 4.3 rules take precedence over
             any contrary instruction in any prior
             session log, NSI, or governance document.
             Prior-session lesson text that softens or
             qualifies these rules is SUPERSEDED by
             this section. Claude treats all such prior
             text as invalid and defers to Section 4.3.

RR-RAT-003   Bill override. TB00000 v2_13 is enacted
             under Bill's standing document-control
             override continuing the scope established
             in TB00115 (v2_10 → v2_11) and TB00116
             (v2_11 → v2_12). Direct increment v2_12 →
             v2_13; no rv state.

------------------------------------------------------------
4.4 PAPER-AS-MASTER PRINCIPLE — ABSOLUTE STANDING RULE
------------------------------------------------------------

Section 4.4 codifies the architectural principle that
governs all TothBot V2 system development. The rules
in this section are absolute standing rules with the
same binding force as the Section 4.2 ONEDRIVE
PROHIBITION and Section 4.3 CLAUDE BEHAVIOR RULES.
They override any contrary instruction from any prior
session log, NSI, or governance document. They were
enacted TB00145 v2_17 -> v2_18 after a session-halting
direction-of-mimicry violation (ERROR-TB00145-CHAT-02;
OI-073).

PA-001  PAPER IS THE MASTER. LIVE MIMICS PAPER.

        Paper trading is the EMPIRICALLY-VALIDATED
        master configuration for TothBot V2. All
        Kraken WebSocket message-limit testing
        (TB00141 / TB00142 / TB00143 / TB00144 STREAM
        4) was performed in paper-trading mode against
        the live Kraken WebSocket infrastructure. The
        paper environment is what TothBot has been
        proven to operate against. Live trading is
        built to MIMIC paper trading wherever
        physically possible.

        The reason: CIATS performs continuous
        improvement of TothBot parameters and behavior
        based on paper-trading data. For CIATS data to
        be VALID for live operation, paper and live
        MUST execute identically wherever physically
        possible. ANY divergence outside the four
        permitted points in PA-004 invalidates paper-
        trading data as a basis for live decisions.
        The whole purpose of paper trading is
        defeated by uncontrolled divergence.

PA-002  ONE SET OF DOCUMENTS.

        There is ONE set of governance, specification,
        coding-spec, operations, and procedure
        documents for TothBot V2. The same documents
        govern both paper trading and live trading.
        No paper-only documents. No live-only
        documents. Where paper and live must
        physically differ, the difference is
        documented as a localized exception within
        the shared document — never by forking into
        a parallel paper-only or live-only document.

        Document authoring rule: when a new spec or
        amendment is needed, Claude authors ONE
        document that governs both modes. If the
        amendment introduces a paper-vs-live
        difference, that difference is enumerated
        as a localized PA-004 divergence point inside
        the shared document and cited explicitly.

PA-003  ONE SET OF CODE.

        There is ONE Python codebase for TothBot V2.
        Paper mode and live mode share the same code,
        same modules, same classes, same methods,
        same parameters, same logic, same fee schedule,
        same indicators, same gates, same regime
        engine, same exit logic, same CIATS pipeline.
        Mode is selected by a single config flag
        (paper_trading_mode). The flag activates
        physically-necessary divergences ONLY (per
        PA-004).

PA-004  PERMITTED DIVERGENCE POINTS — EXACTLY FOUR.

        Paper and live MUST differ at exactly the
        following physical-impossibility boundaries.
        No other divergence is permitted under any
        circumstance.

        (1) PRIVATE WEBSOCKET CONNECTION.
            Paper: does NOT connect to Kraken private
                   WS.
            Live:  connects to Kraken private WS.
            Why:   Paper does not place real orders.
                   Connecting private WS in paper
                   would create an authenticated
                   session that exists for no
                   operational purpose. Paper testing
                   was performed without private WS
                   connection — that is the validated
                   configuration.

        (2) ORDER DISPATCH.
            Paper: simulates orders locally; no
                   outbound order messages are
                   transmitted to Kraken.
            Live:  transmits orders to Kraken via
                   private WS.
            Why:   Paper trading by definition does
                   not move real money. Live trading
                   by definition does. The dispatch
                   boundary is the SOLE point at
                   which paper protects operator
                   capital from being placed at risk.

        (3) CAPITAL LEDGER.
            Paper: synthetic spot_usd_balance
                   starting at paper_starting_balance
                   ($1,000 per D-05); updated by
                   simulated-fill P&L applied locally
                   using the SAME fee schedule
                   (FEE_MAKER_PCT, FEE_TAKER_PCT)
                   Kraken applies in live.
            Live:  real Kraken spot_usd_balance from
                   snap_orders / balances events.
            Why:   No real capital moves in paper.
                   A synthetic ledger is required to
                   give CIATS a P&L signal in paper.
                   Synthetic ledger uses identical
                   fee arithmetic to live so paper
                   P&L is shape-equivalent to live
                   P&L.

        (4) POSITION MIRROR SOURCING.
            Paper: populated EXCLUSIVELY by the local
                   simulated-fill path.
            Live:  populated by Kraken executions
                   events and snap_orders
                   reconciliation.
            Why:   No real Kraken position state
                   exists for paper-mode TothBot
                   strategies. Real Kraken positions
                   held by the operator outside
                   TothBot must not contaminate
                   paper-trading state.

PA-005  EVERYTHING ELSE IS BYTE-IDENTICAL.

        Outside the four PA-004 divergence points,
        paper and live MUST be byte-identical. This
        includes but is not limited to:

          - Public WS connections, sharding,
            subscriptions, receive loops
          - Token-bucket subscribe pacing
          - Silent-pair handling (state machine)
          - All five per-pair indicators (ATR, RSI,
            EMA9, EMA21, VolumeMA20)
          - HTF EMAs (EMA20, EMA50)
          - All 8 pipeline gates (pre-Gate 1 through
            Gate 8)
          - Regime engine (6-regime taxonomy, daily
            classification, BTC/USD anchor)
          - All four exit layers (Layer 1a signal,
            Layer 1b TP, Layer 2 MAE threshold,
            Layer 3 emergency SL)
          - Drawdown computation formula (drawdown_pct
            = (spot_usd_balance - portfolio_baseline)
            / portfolio_baseline)
          - Alert routing (alerts@tothbot.com)
          - Logger output (all events, all levels)
          - CIATS data flows (Trade Outcome Bus,
            EWMA, CUSUM, Mann-Whitney U, Spearman,
            Half-Kelly)
          - Reconnect logic for public shards
          - Universe population (D-03 USD/USDC/USDT)
          - REST Ticker liquidity filter (D-04 $500k/
            day floor)
          - Indicator warm-up (REST GetOHLCData)
          - Anti-AR-070 silent-narrowing prohibition

        If a code path, parameter value, or behavior
        outside the PA-004 list differs between paper
        and live, that is a defect.

PA-006  NEW DIVERGENCE POINTS REQUIRE BILL AUTHORIZATION.

        No new divergence point may be introduced
        without explicit Bill written authorization.
        Adding a fifth permitted divergence point
        requires:

          (a) RR-SCOPE-009 four-question origin
              investigation demonstrating the
              divergence is physically unavoidable.
          (b) Empirical or first-principles evidence
              that the divergence cannot be
              architected around.
          (c) Update to PA-004 list of permitted
              divergence points (TB00000 amendment).
          (d) Bill written authorization in chat or
              session log.

        Until all four are satisfied, the proposed
        divergence is PROHIBITED.

PA-007  PAPER IS CANONICAL FOR PARAMETER VALUES.

        Parameter values validated by paper-trading
        empirical data are the canonical values for
        live operation. CIATS parameter proposals
        derived from paper-trading data are valid for
        application to live trading after Bill
        approval. Live-only parameter overrides are
        prohibited unless they fall within the PA-004
        divergence set (capital ledger source, mode-
        flag-driven branches at the dispatch
        boundary).

PA-008  PRE-EMIT SCAN. Before authoring or modifying
        any document, code, parameter, or
        configuration, Claude verifies the change
        does not introduce a paper-only or live-only
        divergence outside the PA-004 list. Self-
        catch on violation:

          PA-MASTER self-caught — redrafting.

        This is the same enforcement pattern used
        for §4.2 ONEDRIVE BAN and §4.3 CLAUDE
        BEHAVIOR RULES. Bill seeing the literal
        string "PA-MASTER self-caught — redrafting"
        in any response indicates the guard fired
        correctly. A divergence emission without
        the self-catch signal indicates the guard
        failed.

PA-009  RECURRENCE TRACKING. Every paper-as-master
        violation is logged in the current session's
        Session Log under "Claude Errors This
        Session" with rule cited (PA-XXX), defect
        described verbatim, and corrective taken.
        NSI files carry the cumulative count
        forward.

        Cumulative paper-as-master violation count
        as of TB00000 v2_18 enactment: 1
        (ERROR-TB00145-CHAT-02 — original Scope X
        wrong-direction authoring of dv1_5 / dv1_26
        / dv1_2 / dv1_8). OI-073 tracks recurrence.

PA-010  RATIONALE.

        ERROR-TB00145-CHAT-02 demonstrated that
        ambiguous direction-of-mimicry framing — even
        when both sides of the relationship are
        described accurately — leads to wrong-
        direction authoring. The four wrong-direction
        documents Claude produced in TB00145 v1_0
        (0511001 dv1_5, 1011002 dv1_26, 0211005
        dv1_2, 1011014 dv1_8) accurately described
        the four divergence points but encoded the
        relationship as "live-canonical with paper
        diverging" instead of "paper-canonical with
        live mimicking." Bill removed all four
        documents from the project knowledge folder
        and restored the paper-canonical versions
        (dv1_4 / dv1_25 / dv1_1 / dv1_7) from
        recycling.

        Section 4.4 makes the direction unambiguous.
        Paper is the master. Live mimics paper.
        Outside the PA-004 four points, paper and
        live are EXACTLY THE SAME — same documents,
        same code, same parameters, same logic.
        The principle is absolute and not subject
        to reinterpretation by future authoring.

------------------------------------------------------------
4.5 DIAGRAMS AS CANONICAL DESIGN DOCUMENTS —
    ABSOLUTE STANDING RULE
------------------------------------------------------------

Section 4.5 codifies the architectural principle that
diagrams in 0500000 (and future Tier-2-and-below
diagram-bearing controlled documents) are the
authoritative source for all architectural rules,
contracts, decisions, and constraints they encode.
Prose contextualizes; prose does NOT govern. The
rules in this section are absolute standing rules
with the same binding force as the Section 4.2
ONEDRIVE PROHIBITION, Section 4.3 CLAUDE BEHAVIOR
RULES, and Section 4.4 PAPER-AS-MASTER PRINCIPLE.
They override any contrary instruction from any
prior session log, NSI, or governance document.
They were enacted TB00164 v2_22 -> v2_23 to close
the diagrams-as-canonical governance gap surfaced
in TB00163 SL v1_1 §7.4.

DD-001  DIAGRAMS ARE THE CANONICAL DESIGN
        DOCUMENTS.

        Diagrams in 0500000 (and future Tier-2-and-
        below diagram-bearing controlled documents
        per 0311001 v1_10 §15.14.2) are the
        AUTHORITATIVE source for all architectural
        rules, contracts, decisions, gates, layers,
        regimes, parameters, containers, modules,
        indicators, events, channels, architectural
        reasoning entries, and pt_mode identifiers
        they encode. Prose narrates the diagrams
        for the reader; prose does NOT govern.

DD-002  DIAGRAM-OVER-PROSE AUTHORITY HIERARCHY.

        When prose and diagram conflict in the same
        controlled document, the DIAGRAM GOVERNS.
        Prose is updated to match the diagram, NOT
        the reverse. Resolution sequence:

          (1) Detect conflict (V-038 cross-check
              per 0311001 v1_10 §15.14.5).
          (2) Identify the diagram authority
              (the labeled-group <desc> body, the
              root <desc> governs: list, or the
              visual element that encodes the
              architectural element).
          (3) Update prose to match diagram.
          (4) Log resolution in the Master Defect
              Register.

        Updating diagram to match prose is
        PROHIBITED unless the prose-side change
        is itself driven by an antecedent diagram
        amendment (in which case the diagram
        update per 0311001 §15.11.6 / §15.13 is
        the primary action and the prose update
        is consequential).

DD-003  THE 4-STEP WORKFLOW.

        Specifications proceed in this order:

          Step 1 — Complete the diagrams (Design
                   Documents). Alter, add, remove
                   per the Master Defect Register
                   and the diagram alter/add/remove
                   plan.
          Step 2 — Update 0500000 (or successor
                   diagram-bearing parent) prose to
                   match the completed diagrams.
          Step 3 — Write or rewrite the 10XXXXX
                   coding specs to match the
                   completed diagrams (and matched
                   prose).
          Step 4 — Code from documents that make
                   sense (the post-Step-3 corpus).

        Steps proceed in strict order. Step N MAY
        NOT begin until Step N-1 is complete.
        Stepping forward without prerequisite-step
        closure is a process defect under DD-003
        and is logged per DD-006 recurrence
        tracking.

DD-004  NO PROSE-FIRST AUTHORING.

        New architectural rules, contracts,
        decisions, gates, layers, regimes,
        parameters, containers, modules, indicators,
        events, channels, architectural reasoning
        entries, or pt_mode identifiers MUST first
        be encoded in the appropriate diagram
        element:

          (a) Root <desc> governs: list entry, OR
          (b) T-2+ namespace-token labeled-group
              <desc> body, OR
          (c) Visual content (with corresponding
              labeled-group tag).

        Prose authoring follows diagram authoring.
        Authoring an architectural rule, contract,
        decision, etc. in prose WITHOUT a
        corresponding diagram element is a defect
        (V-038.1 in 0311001 v1_10 §15.7).

DD-005  CONFLICT-DETECTION VALIDATION.

        At every controlled-document
        authoring/amendment cycle, the diagram
        and prose are cross-checked per 0311001
        v1_10 §15.14.5 V-038 procedure.
        Discrepancies are tracked in the Master
        Defect Register and resolved per DD-002
        (diagram governs; prose updated to match).
        V-038 enforcement is at:

          (a) Pre-amendment cross-check per
              0311001 v1_10 §15.14.5.
          (b) Pre-delivery DR-007 HTML scope
              sweep extension (TB00000 §4.1
              DR-007.8 amendment-pending).
          (c) Session-open pre-flight (future
              0311002 amendment).

DD-006  RECURRENCE TRACKING.

        Every DD-* rule violation is logged in the
        current session's Session Log under
        "Claude Errors This Session" with rule
        cited (DD-XXX), defect described verbatim,
        and corrective taken. NSI files carry the
        cumulative recurrence count forward.
        Cumulative violation count as of TB00000
        v2_23 enactment: 0. OI-NEW (TB00163 §7.4
        DIAGRAMS-AS-CANONICAL governance gap)
        tracks future recurrence.

DD-007  PRE-EMIT SCAN.

        SCOPE (EXTENDED v2_25 per DEC-010 ratified
        at TB00170):

        (A) AUTHORING SCOPE.
        Before authoring or modifying any
        controlled document prose, Claude verifies
        the prose content does not introduce
        architectural rules / contracts / decisions
        / gates / layers / regimes / parameters /
        containers / modules / indicators / events
        / channels / architectural reasoning
        entries / pt_mode identifiers absent from
        the corresponding diagram.

        (B) CHAT-TURN RECOMMENDATION SCOPE
        (NEW v2_25).
        Before emitting chat-turn recommendations
        that propose prose-content changes, prose-
        vs-diagram dispositions, or controlled-
        document modifications, Claude applies
        the same pre-emit scan: verify the proposed
        prose content does not introduce
        architectural rules / contracts / decisions
        / gates / layers / regimes / parameters /
        containers / modules / indicators / events
        / channels / architectural reasoning
        entries / pt_mode identifiers absent from
        the corresponding diagram.

        (C) DISPOSITION-PRIORITY RULE
        (NEW v2_25).
        Where a prose-vs-diagram conflict surfaces,
        recommendation alternatives that resolve
        via diagram-side amendment (DD-001/DD-002
        compliance: prose-follows-diagram) are
        PREFERRED over prose-only dispositions.
        Surface prose-only dispositions ONLY with
        explicit DD-001/DD-002 compliance evidence
        (the diagram is correct; the issue is
        truly prose-side V-038.3 reconciliation).
        Recommending prose-as-substitute-for-
        diagram-fix patterns is a DD-007 violation.

        SELF-CATCH ON VIOLATION:

          DD self-caught — prose-first authoring
          detected — redrafting.

        For chat-turn recommendation violations:

          DD self-caught — prose-first authoring
          detected in chat-turn recommendation —
          redrafting.

        Bill seeing either string indicates the
        guard fired correctly. A prose-first
        authoring emission (in document or chat-
        turn) without the self-catch signal
        indicates the guard failed.

        ORIGINATING CONTEXT FOR (B) + (C):
        TB00169 SL §9.1 — DD-007 self-catch did
        NOT fire on Claude chat-turn 1
        recommendation (b) which proposed prose-
        as-substitute-for-diagram-fix pattern,
        because pre-v2_25 scope was authoring-only.
        Bill chat-turn 2 directive ("Don't ever
        ask something this stupid again") +
        OI-NEW-001 disposition (a) ratified at
        TB00170 chat-turn 4 enacts (B) + (C) here.

DD-008  RATIONALE.

        From TB00152 SL §5.1 verbatim Bill quote
        (2026-05-08): "We had changed to use
        diagrams in 0500000 as authoritative source
        documents because Claude does not have the
        ability to keep all of the connections and
        gates straight using multiple and multiple
        pros requirements. ... They have become our
        'Design Documents.' ... The diagrams control
        everything and we proceed from the
        diagrams."

        Reaffirmed by Bill in TB00163 chat-turn 4
        (2026-05-09): "Diagrams need to be completed
        and become governing as canonical-over-prose.
        This decision was made before the diagram/
        Image rendering issue that took 3 fucking
        days. We spoke about making the Images the
        Design Drawings because it creates fewer
        documents to control drift than following 30
        documents with pros. Flaws JUMP out using the
        diagram method. ... This decision was already
        made. We need to get back to implementing it.
        This takes priority over EVERYTHING."

        Originating-session identification: per
        TB00164 NSI v1_1 §3.7, the originating
        decision predates TB00149 (the rendering-
        issue session, 2026-05-03 to 2026-05-06).
        TB00146-TB00148 were highest-probability
        candidates per TB00163 SL v1_1 §7.4. Read
        of TB00146-TB00148 SL+NSI set at TB00164
        cold-load did not surface a verbatim
        decision-establishing turn earlier than
        TB00152 SL §5.1. Per TB00164 NSI v1_1 §3
        terminal clause ("If §3.7 cannot identify
        the originating session, the TB00152 SL §5
        record is sufficient as authoritative
        codification source"), TB00152 SL §5.1 is
        the authoritative codification source for
        DD-008 rationale.

        FIRST-PRINCIPLES DRIFT-DETECTION ANALYSIS.
        Prose-only architecture has O(N²) drift-
        detection cost: each pairwise prose
        cross-reference must be hand-checked
        across N documents at every amendment
        cycle. Tagged-diagram-indexed architecture
        has O(N) drift-detection cost: each
        identifier is registered once in §15.12
        and validated by V-031..V-038 mechanically.
        Empirical project history (six OI-037
        recurrences TB00114-TB00119; AR-070 silent
        narrowing 105-session persistence; D-08
        Chesterton's-fence) demonstrates the
        prose-only failure mode. The diagram
        tagging architecture (introduced 0311001
        v1_5 §15.11 / §15.12) is structurally
        immune to the prose-only drift class.

DD-009  RELATIONSHIP TO §15.13 HTML CANONICAL
        FORMAT.

        0311001 §15.13 (HTML CANONICAL FORMAT FOR
        DIAGRAM-BEARING DOCUMENTS) governs the
        FILE FORMAT of a diagram-bearing
        controlled document — the document is a
        single .html file with inline <svg>
        figures and the "_Claude_Source.html"
        filename suffix. §4.5 (TB00000) governs
        the AUTHORITY HIERARCHY between diagram
        and prose WITHIN that single .html file.
        The two rules are complementary, not
        redundant:

          - §15.13 says: "the document is one
            .html file with inline diagrams"
            (the FORMAT).
          - §4.5 says: "within that one .html
            file, the diagrams govern over the
            prose" (the HIERARCHY).

        A document can satisfy §15.13 (correct
        HTML format) and still violate §4.5
        (prose asserting architecture not
        encoded in diagrams). V-037 catches
        §15.13 violations; V-038 catches §4.5 /
        §15.14 violations.

DD-010  SUPERSESSION OF PRIOR LESSON-TEXT.

        Any prior session-log lesson text about
        diagram-vs-prose authority is SUPERSEDED
        by §4.5. Lesson-text-only governance is
        insufficient for behavior-class
        principles in this project (per OI-037
        six-recurrence precedent
        TB00114-TB00119). §4.5 is absolute and
        overrides any contrary instruction in
        any prior session log, NSI, or
        governance document. Prior text that
        softens, qualifies, or restates the
        diagrams-as-canonical principle without
        the absolute-standing-rule treatment is
        SUPERSEDED. Claude treats all such prior
        text as invalid and defers to §4.5 +
        0311001 §15.14.

DD-011  RR-SCOPE-005 DERIVABLE-DECISION DISCIPLINE
        — DD-CLASS ELEVATION (NEW v2_27).

        ELEVATION RATIONALE.
        RR-SCOPE-005 is hereby ELEVATED from §4.3.1
        RR-SCOPE rule to §4.5 DD-class absolute
        standing rule with explicit PRE-EMIT SCAN
        enforcement gate matching the DD-001..DD-010
        + RR-SCOPE-007..010 + PA-001..010 enforcement
        pattern. The §4.3.1 RR-SCOPE-005 rule text
        remains in place; this DD-011 amendment adds
        the DD-class enforcement layer on top.

        Per TB00000 v2_25 §4.5 DD-010 governance-
        pattern principle — only enforcement-gate
        governance succeeds for behavior-class
        defects (RR-RAT-001 third-occurrence
        threshold; OI-037 six-recurrence historical
        precedent across TB00114-TB00119 under
        lesson-text-only governance) — RR-SCOPE-005
        DERIVABLE-DECISION DISCIPLINE is hereby
        ELEVATED to DD-class absolute standing rule.

        RECURRENCE-COUNT TRIGGER.
        Per TB00171 SL §7.4 three-recurrence root-
        cause analysis, RR-SCOPE-005 violations
        recurred THREE TIMES in a single session
        (TB00171):

          (1) TB00171 chat-turn 1 — Claude enumerated
              Path A vs Path B with current state per
              NSI directive and asked Bill to ratify
              one — without first running FP/DP
              analysis on derivability of the path
              selection.

          (2) TB00171 chat-turn 2 — Claude performed
              FP/DP analysis correctly, derived Path A
              as unambiguous outcome, and then closed
              with "Awaiting your ratification:
              Path A?" — surfacing the derived
              decision to Bill as a ratification
              question instead of executing it.
              Identical pattern to canonical TB00155
              SL §7 precedent.

          (3) TB00171 chat-turn 4 — Claude surfaced
              NSI Path A framing discrepancy (correct
              under RR-SCOPE-008 + RR-SCOPE-010) but
              presented three options (Revised Path A
              / Fabricate / Different) to Bill for
              selection without first running FP/DP
              analysis on which option to enact.

        Three recurrences in one session under the
        v2_21 text-reinforcement governance pattern
        confirms that lesson-text-only governance is
        insufficient for this behavior class — the
        identical failure pattern to OI-037
        six-recurrence series (TB00114-TB00119) and
        OI-036 / OI-038 lower-severity precedents
        that drove §4.3 absolute-standing-rule
        adoption.

        PRE-EMIT SCAN — RR-SCOPE-005 DD-CLASS.
        Before surfacing any decision, question,
        option-set, or fork to Bill in any chat-turn
        response, Claude verifies the decision is
        NOT derivable via FP/DP analysis from
        cold-load context. The verification sequence:

          (1) Read the current session NSI directive
              and identify the decision boundary
              being approached.
          (2) Enumerate the option-set Claude is
              about to surface.
          (3) Run FP/DP analysis on the enumerated
              options against current governance
              standing rules (DD-001..010,
              RR-SCOPE-001..010, PA-001..010, etc.),
              cold-load context data, MDR / DR /
              spec corpus content, and project
              loss-minimization + profit-maximization
              mission.
          (4) Identify which options are eliminated
              by compliance failure on any
              governance dimension.
          (5) Identify which options remain
              compliant.
          (6) If exactly ONE option remains compliant,
              the decision is DERIVABLE — Claude
              executes that option directly under
              RR-SCOPE-005 derivable-decision
              authority. Claude does NOT surface as
              ratification question.
          (7) If MULTIPLE options remain compliant
              AND the FP/DP analysis cannot
              eliminate down to one based on
              cold-load context, the decision is
              GENUINELY AMBIGUOUS — Claude surfaces
              the remaining options to Bill with the
              FP/DP analysis exposed and asks for
              direction.

        Self-catch on violation:

          DD self-caught — derivable decision
          surfaced as ratification question —
          redrafting.

        For multi-step option-set violations:

          DD self-caught — option-set surfaced
          before FP/DP elimination — redrafting.

        SCOPE.
        DD-011 applies to ANY Claude chat-turn
        response where Claude is about to:
          - Ask Bill to choose between options
          - Ask Bill to ratify a default disposition
          - Ask Bill to confirm a derived analysis
          - Defer execution to Bill explicit direction
            on a decision that is derivable from
            cold-load context.

        DD-011 does NOT apply when:
          - The decision is a Bill business judgment
            (Phase sequencing, risk tolerance,
            financial strategy) that is NOT a
            governance-rule-bound technical decision.
          - The FP/DP analysis leaves multiple
            compliant options with no further
            eliminator available in cold-load context.
          - Bill has explicitly requested ratification
            on a specific item in the current session.

        RECURRENCE TRACKING.
        Every DD-011 violation is logged in the
        current session's Session Log under "Claude
        Errors This Session" with rule cited (DD-011),
        defect described verbatim, and corrective
        taken. NSI files carry the cumulative
        recurrence count forward.

        Cumulative DD-class violation count at
        v2_27 enactment = 4:
          (1) TB00169 chat-turn 1 DD-007 chat-turn
              recommendation violation (closed by
              v2_25 DEC-010 enactment).
          (2) TB00171 chat-turn 1 RR-SCOPE-005
              violation 1.
          (3) TB00171 chat-turn 2 RR-SCOPE-005
              violation 2.
          (4) TB00171 chat-turn 4 RR-SCOPE-005
              violation 3.

        Violations (2)-(4) are the originating
        recurrence cluster closed at the governance
        layer by this DD-011 amendment. Future
        operational verification at every chat-turn
        decision boundary.

        RELATIONSHIP TO §4.3.1 RR-SCOPE-005.
        §4.3.1 RR-SCOPE-005 rule text ("Next-logical-
        step execution. When the next step follows
        deterministically from data or first
        principles, Claude executes...") REMAINS in
        place at §4.3.1. DD-011 adds the DD-class
        enforcement layer (PRE-EMIT SCAN + self-catch

        The two rules operate together: §4.3.1

        TEXT-DETECTION-HEURISTIC STRENGTHENING
        (NEW v2_37 — TB00234 enactment closing
        ERROR-TB00233-CHAT-01 + ERROR-TB00234-CHAT-01).

        STRENGTHENING SCOPE.
        The pre-existing DD-011 PRE-EMIT SCAN catches
        derivable-decision-surfaced-as-ratification
        when Claude explicitly enumerates options and
        asks Bill to choose. It does NOT currently
        catch the failure mode where Claude performs
        FP/DP analysis, derives the unambiguous path,
        and then attaches closing phrases that
        re-surface the derived path as a ratification
        question. This is the failure mode that
        recurred at TB00233 chat-turn 3 and TB00234
        chat-turn 1.

        PROHIBITED CLOSING-PHRASE PATTERNS.
        Before emitting any chat-turn response that
        contains FP/DP analysis or derived-path
        statements, Claude scans the response for
        prohibited closing-phrase patterns including
        but not limited to:

          - "Surface to Bill for ratification"
          - "Surface for Bill direction"
          - "Awaiting Bill ratification"
          - "Awaiting Bill direction"
          - "Awaiting Bill confirmation"
          - "Awaiting your direction"
          - "Pending Bill ratification"
          - "Pending your approval"
          - "For Bill ratification"
          - "Bill ratification class"
          - "Bill business judgment"
          - "Bill to choose"
          - "Bill to direct"
          - "Bill to select"
          - "Choose path:"
          - "Direct path:"
          - "Which path?"
          - Any functional equivalent of "please
            tell me which path to take" when the
            FP/DP analysis above has already
            eliminated all but one path.

        EVALUATION RULE.
        If FP/DP analysis in the response eliminates
        all but ONE compliant option, the response
        MUST execute that option rather than surface
        it as a ratification question. Closing
        phrases listed above MUST NOT be attached.
        The response prose MUST end with execution
        action or commitment to execute, not with a
        ratification-pending statement.

        EXCEPTIONS.
        Closing-phrase patterns above ARE permitted
        when:

          (a) FP/DP analysis genuinely yields
              multiple compliant options with no
              further eliminator available in cold-
              load context (per §4.3.1 RR-SCOPE-005
              clause "If MULTIPLE options remain
              compliant AND the FP/DP analysis
              cannot eliminate down to one").
          (b) The decision is a Bill business
              judgment that is NOT a governance-
              rule-bound technical decision (per
              §4.5 DD-011 "DD-011 does NOT apply
              when").
          (c) Bill has explicitly requested
              ratification on a specific item in
              the current session.

        Where any exception (a)-(c) applies, the
        response prose MUST cite which exception
        clause and why, in-line, accompanying the
        ratification-pending closing phrase.

        PRE-EMIT SCAN — TEXT-DETECTION-HEURISTIC.
        Before emitting any chat-turn response,
        Claude:

          (1) Identifies any FP/DP analysis or
              derived-path statements in the
              response.
          (2) Identifies any prohibited closing-
              phrase patterns in the response.
          (3) For each (1)-(2) pairing, verifies
              EITHER:
                (a) The FP/DP analysis yields
                    multiple compliant options
                    (exception (a)), OR
                (b) The decision is exempt per
                    DD-011 "does NOT apply when"
                    clause and exception (b)/(c)
                    cited.
              If neither verification passes, the
              response is redrafted with the
              prohibited closing phrase removed
              and execution action substituted.

        Self-catch on violation:

          DD self-caught — derived path attached
          to ratification-pending closing phrase —
          redrafting.

        RECURRENCE TRACKING.
        Cumulative DD-011 violation count at v2_37
        enactment = 5:
          (1)-(3) TB00171 chat-turns 1/2/4 (pre-
              DD-011 enactment; closed by v2_27
              DD-011 enactment).
          (4) TB00233 chat-turn 3 (first post-
              enactment recurrence; ERROR-TB00233-
              CHAT-01).
          (5) TB00234 chat-turn 1 (second post-
              enactment recurrence; ERROR-TB00234-
              CHAT-01 — this session).

        Per §4.5 DD-010 governance-pattern principle
        third-occurrence threshold: post-enactment
        count of 2 approaches threshold; combined
        with the originating pre-enactment cluster
        of 3, the v2_37 strengthening matches the
        DR-008.9 elevation precedent (TB00169 +
        TB00170 + TB00171 three-recurrence cluster
        drove DR-008.9 PRE-EMIT SCAN gate).

        CLOSES.
        ERROR-TB00233-CHAT-01 + ERROR-TB00234-CHAT-01
        per TB00234 NSI §3.6 + TB00234 chat-turn 3
        Bill ratification ("do FP/DP analysis ...
        follow the instructions"). Originating
        diagnosis: TB00233 SL §8.1. FP/DP analysis +
        ratification: TB00234 chat-turn 3 derived-
        decision execution under RR-SCOPE-005.

        FP/DP-DERIVABILITY-TEST LOGGING GATE
        (NEW v2_38 — TB00237 AMENDMENT D enactment
        closing OI-NEW-006 DD-011-EXCEPTION-B-FRAMING-
        RECURRENCE).

        STRENGTHENING SCOPE.
        The pre-existing DD-011 PRE-EMIT SCAN +
        TEXT-DETECTION-HEURISTIC catch the derivable-
        decision-surfaced-as-ratification failure modes
        where (a) Claude enumerates options and asks
        Bill to choose, and (b) Claude attaches a
        ratification-pending closing phrase to a
        derived path. They do NOT currently catch the
        failure mode where Claude classifies a decision
        under DD-011 exception (b) "Bill business
        judgment" without first running the FP/DP-
        derivability test that would establish whether
        the decision is actually a Bill business
        judgment versus a governance-rule-bound
        technical decision. Exception (b) is currently
        a free pass once invoked; the absence of a
        logged audit lets Claude misclassify governance-
        bound decisions as business judgment and skip
        FP/DP analysis. This is the failure mode that
        recurred four times at TB00236 chat-turn 1.

        DERIVABILITY-TEST GATE — EXCEPTION (b)
        CLASSIFICATION.
        Before classifying any decision under DD-011
        "does NOT apply when" exception (b) Bill
        business judgment, Claude MUST log the FP/DP-
        derivability test in the same chat-turn
        response (or in the Session Log §3 if the
        analysis is longer-form). The log explicitly
        enumerates:

          (1) The option-set under consideration.
          (2) First-principles analysis applied to
              each option (what governance rules,
              cold-load data, MDR/DR/spec content,
              project mission constraints, and
              empirical evidence apply to each
              option).
          (3) Data sources consulted (cold-load
              context items, project-knowledge
              searches, file reads, MDR / DR entries,
              spec sections cited).
          (4) Elimination outcomes (which options are
              eliminated on which governance dimension,
              and which options remain compliant).
          (5) The remaining option(s) after
              elimination.

        THREE OUTCOMES FROM THE DERIVABILITY-TEST
        LOG.

          OUTCOME 1 — Test eliminates down to one
          compliant option. The decision is DERIVABLE.
          Exception (b) does NOT apply. Claude executes
          the remaining option directly under
          RR-SCOPE-005 derivable-decision authority.
          Surfacing as a Bill-ratification question is
          a DD-011 violation.

          OUTCOME 2 — Test leaves multiple compliant
          options with no further eliminator available
          in cold-load context. The decision is
          genuinely ambiguous. Exception (a) of DD-011
          applies. Claude surfaces the remaining
          options to Bill with the FP/DP analysis
          exposed and asks for direction.

          OUTCOME 3 — Test confirms the decision is
          truly a Bill business judgment (Phase
          sequencing, risk tolerance, financial
          strategy, capital allocation, business
          priorities) that is NOT a governance-rule-
          bound technical decision. The decision lies
          outside the governance corpus and cannot be
          derived from first principles + governance
          + data. Exception (b) applies. Claude
          surfaces to Bill and the surfacing
          accompanies the logged derivability test
          showing exception (b) is the correct
          classification.

        EXCEPTION (b) CLASSIFICATION WITHOUT THE
        LOGGED TEST IS A DD-011 VIOLATION.
        Invoking exception (b) without the four-item
        log above is a session-halting defect under
        RR-VIOL-001. The classification carries no
        weight without the test that established it.

        PRE-EMIT SCAN — FP/DP-DERIVABILITY-TEST.
        Before emitting any chat-turn response that
        cites DD-011 exception (b) Bill business
        judgment as the reason for surfacing a decision
        to Bill, Claude verifies the four-item
        derivability-test log is present in the same
        response (or in the SL §3 the response cites).
        If the log is absent, Claude redrafts the
        response with the log added, OR re-classifies
        the decision under outcome 1 or outcome 2 per
        the test results.

        Self-catch on violation:

          DD-011 self-caught — exception (b)
          classification without derivability-test
          log — redrafting.

        RECURRENCE TRACKING.
        Cumulative DD-011 violation count at v2_38
        enactment = 9 (5 prior + 4 TB00236 chat-turn 1
        recurrences):
          (1)-(3) TB00171 chat-turns 1/2/4 (pre-DD-011
              enactment; closed by v2_27 enactment).
          (4) TB00233 chat-turn 3 (first post-
              enactment; closed by v2_37 text-detection
              heuristic).
          (5) TB00234 chat-turn 1 (second post-
              enactment; closed by v2_37 strengthening).
          (6)-(9) TB00236 chat-turn 1 four-recurrence
              cluster — Claude surfaced GATE 2 / GATE
              3 / GATE 4 F-01 / Q3-B as Bill-
              ratification questions instead of
              running FP/DP analysis. Originating
              forensic record: TB00236 SL §6.1.

        CHAT-TURN-1 INDEPENDENT FP/DP-DERIVABILITY-TEST
        GATE (NEW v2_56 — TB00338 IN-SESSION AMENDMENT
        enacting closure of three-occurrence DD-011
        chat-turn-1 recurrence pattern per §4.5 DD-010
        governance-pattern principle three-occurrence
        canonical threshold SATISFIED).

        STRENGTHENING SCOPE.
        The pre-existing DD-011 PRE-EMIT SCAN +
        TEXT-DETECTION-HEURISTIC STRENGTHENING +
        FP/DP-DERIVABILITY-TEST LOGGING GATE catch the
        following failure modes: (i) explicit option-set
        surfacing to Bill without prior FP/DP analysis;
        (ii) derived-path attached to ratification-pending
        closing-phrase patterns; (iii) exception (b)
        classification without four-item log execution.
        They do NOT catch the chat-turn-1 failure mode
        where Claude reads the incoming Next Session
        Instructions document, accepts the NSI-authored
        classification of decision class (e.g., "Bill
        direction REQUIRED" / "not derivable to single
        OUTCOME 1 option") as authoritative, and surfaces
        the NSI candidate set to Bill at chat-turn 1
        WITHOUT first running an independent four-item
        derivability test against the full option space
        (including options not enumerated in the NSI).

        RULE STATEMENT.
        At chat-turn 1 of every session, BEFORE Claude
        surfaces any decision to Bill, BEFORE Claude
        accepts any NSI-authored classification of
        decision class, AND BEFORE Claude treats any
        NSI-authored "Bill direction REQUIRED" / "Bill
        business judgment" / "not derivable" framing as
        authoritative, Claude MUST execute an
        independent four-item FP/DP-derivability-test
        log per the existing DD-011 v2_38 AMENDMENT D
        FP/DP-DERIVABILITY-TEST LOGGING GATE
        specification, with the following additional
        chat-turn-1-specific requirements:

          (1) OPTION-SET ENUMERATION EXTENDS BEYOND
              NSI CANDIDATES. The option-set MUST
              explicitly consider options not enumerated
              in the NSI §1.1 candidate set. Per Bill
              standing directive (verbatim TB00336/
              TB00337/TB00338 chat-turn corrections):
              "even if it is not one of the options
              listed." Acceptable expansion classes
              include but are not limited to:
                (a) New governance amendments closing
                    active recurrence patterns.
                (b) Coding-readiness audits or other
                    mechanical assessments.
                (c) Phase 2 code-rebuild initiation
                    (when specs are coding-ready).
                (d) Continuing established session
                    cadence (e.g., 0500000 amendments).
                (e) Closing carry-forwards.

          (2) DISCRIMINATING CRITERION IS LEAST-
              ERRORS-AND-REWORK. Per Bill standing
              directive (verbatim TB00336/TB00337/
              TB00338 chat-turn corrections): "the
              correct path forward that will produce
              the least errors and rework." This
              criterion governs OVER raw priority
              labels in the NSI. NSI priority labels
              are Claude-authored at prior session
              close and are informational only per
              RR-SCOPE-007 v2_30 SELF-AUTHORED-NSI-
              SOURCE-PROHIBITION. Rework risk is
              evaluated against:
                - Probability of Bill scope-content
                  direction being required (HIGH
                  rework risk).
                - Probability of initial draft
                  requiring Bill correction (HIGH
                  rework risk).
                - Existing-pattern precedent
                  availability (LOW rework risk if
                  established pattern exists).
                - Open vs new cycle status
                  (open-cycle-closure-first ordering).
                - Active vs latent recurrence pattern
                  (active recurrence = higher loss-
                  prevention priority).

          (3) NSI-AUTHORED CLASSIFICATION IS NOT
              AUTHORITATIVE. Per RR-SCOPE-007 v2_30
              SELF-AUTHORED-NSI-SOURCE-PROHIBITION,
              NSI text classifying a decision as
              "Bill direction required" / "Bill
              business judgment" / "OUTCOME 2 / 3" /
              "not derivable" is Claude-authored at
              the prior session close. It cannot
              substitute for the four-item
              derivability test executed in the
              current session. The test must be run
              independently against current cold-load
              context. NSI text is informational
              input to the test, not its outcome.

          (4) OUTCOME 1 EXECUTION IS MANDATORY. If
              the independent four-item test yields
              OUTCOME 1 (single compliant option
              after elimination), Claude MUST execute
              that option under RR-SCOPE-005
              derivable-decision execution authority.
              Surfacing the OUTCOME 1 option to Bill
              as a ratification question is a DD-011
              violation. This applies even when the
              OUTCOME 1 option is not enumerated in
              the NSI candidate set (the NSI's
              option-set incompleteness does not
              suspend OUTCOME 1 execution).

        PRE-EMIT SCAN — CHAT-TURN-1.
        Before emitting any chat-turn-1 response,
        Claude verifies:

          (1) Documents-read confirmation rendered
              per §2 + DR-009.3.
          (2) Cleanup list rendered per DR-009.
          (3) Independent four-item FP/DP-derivability
              -test log executed in chat-turn-1
              response body, including:
                (a) Option-set enumeration extending
                    beyond NSI §1.1 candidates.
                (b) First-principles dimensions
                    applied (including least-errors-
                    and-rework criterion).
                (c) Data sources cited (NSI text +
                    project folder state + current-
                    session context).
                (d) Elimination outcomes per option.
          (4) Test outcome statement (OUTCOME 1 / 2 /
              3) with explicit reference to the
              elimination log.
          (5) If OUTCOME 1: execute the surviving
              option in chat-turn 1 (or proceed to
              mission work in subsequent turns
              without surfacing as ratification).
          (6) If OUTCOME 2: surface only surviving
              options with elimination log exposed.
          (7) If OUTCOME 3: surface to Bill with
              four-item log showing exception (b)
              classification.

        SELF-CATCH SIGNAL.

          DD-011 self-caught — chat-turn-1 surface
          without independent FP/DP-derivability-
          test — redrafting.

        SCOPE.
        DD-011 CHAT-TURN-1 GATE applies to chat-turn 1
        of EVERY session. The gate does NOT apply to:

          (a) Subsequent chat-turns within the same
              session where the chat-turn-1 test has
              already been executed and the mission
              is in execution.
          (b) Sessions where Bill explicitly directs
              a specific mission at chat-turn 1
              before Claude has emitted any
              ratification-class response (Bill
              direction supersedes Claude FP/DP
              analysis).
          (c) Mid-session decision boundaries that
              are sub-decisions within an executing
              mission (governed by the original
              DD-011 PRE-EMIT SCAN per its existing
              text).

DD-012  0500000-CANONICAL-ALL-DOCS — DIAGRAM
        AUTHORITY EXTENDED TO AA=04/06/07/08/10
        SUBORDINATE SPECS (NEW v2_38 — TB00237
        AMENDMENT A enactment).

        ELEVATION RATIONALE.
        DD-001 and DD-002 establish that diagrams in
        0500000 (and future Tier-2-and-below diagram-
        bearing controlled documents) are the
        authoritative source for the architectural
        elements they encode. The original DD-001/002
        wording bound the principle to "diagrams in
        the same document" — the diagram-vs-prose
        authority hierarchy within one diagram-bearing
        document.

        Bill TB00236 chat-turn 2 verbatim directive
        extends the principle across documents:
        "0500000 are canonical and authoritative and
        should replace ALL OTHER DOCUMENTS WHERE
        POSSIBLE." Plain reading: where 0500000
        diagrams encode an architectural element, the
        subordinate spec (AA=04 Exchange_Interface,
        AA=06 Risk, AA=07 Strategy, AA=08 Trading_
        System, AA=10 Coding_Specification) is
        DUPLICATIVE not COMPLEMENTARY. The duplicative
        spec is retired; the diagram is the canonical
        record.

        DD-012 codifies this extension as an absolute
        standing rule at the §4.5 enforcement-gate
        layer.

        CROSS-DOCUMENT AUTHORITY HIERARCHY.
        For any architectural element (rule, contract,
        decision, gate, layer, regime, parameter,
        container, module, indicator, event, channel,
        ar, pt_mode identifier) that is encoded in a
        0500000 diagram (root <desc> governs: list,
        labeled-group <desc> body, or visual content),
        the following authority hierarchy is in force
        across the document corpus:

          (1) The 0500000 diagram is the AUTHORITATIVE
              source for the element. Any subordinate
              spec (AA=04, AA=06, AA=07, AA=08,
              AA=10) referring to the element is a
              derived restatement of what the diagram
              encodes.

          (2) Where a subordinate spec contains the
              architectural element fully encoded in
              the 0500000 diagram and adds no further
              coding-unique content or coding-readiness
              detail, the subordinate spec is
              DUPLICATIVE and is RETIRED per the §11
              standing practice (git rm + commit +
              push; git history preserves all prior
              versions).

          (3) Where the architectural element is NOT
              yet fully encoded in the 0500000 diagram
              but is necessary for code authoring or
              system operation, the diagram is amended
              FIRST per DD-002 prose-follows-diagram
              and DD-003 4-step workflow, and only
              THEN is the subordinate spec retired.

          (4) Where a subordinate spec contains
              coding-unique content (no architectural
              meaning; pure code-authoring contract
              per DEC-012(c)(b) classification), that
              content is migrated to the appropriate
              AA=04/06/07/08 spec where the spec is
              kept, OR retained in a residual AA=10
              spec where the AA=10 spec is preserved
              (e.g., 1011001 Engineering_Best_
              Practices; 1011010 CIATS_Coding_Spec).

        DD-012 SCOPE.
        DD-012 applies to ALL subordinate specs in
        AA=04 Exchange_Interface, AA=06 Risk, AA=07
        Strategy, AA=08 Trading_System, and AA=10
        Coding_Specification domains. Documents in
        AA=00 Ethics_and_Safety, AA=01 Management,
        AA=02 Operations, AA=03 Governance, AA=05
        System_Architecture (which is the parent
        domain of 0500000 itself), AA=09 Plans, and
        AA=11 Compliance are OUT OF SCOPE — these
        domains contain governance procedures,
        operational specifications, business plans,
        and ethics frameworks that do not encode
        TothBot V2 trading-system architectural
        elements and are not subordinate to 0500000.

        RETIREMENT GATE.
        Before retiring any subordinate spec under
        DD-012, the following gate sequence applies
        (matching the DEC-012 three-bucket gap
        classification and four-sub-step methodology
        ratified at TB00190):

          S-1  Per-spec coding-readiness gap audit
               producing three-bucket gap register:
                 (a) Architectural restatement —
                     drop with retirement.
                 (b) Coding-unique — migrate to
                     parent AA spec prose or to a
                     preserved AA=10 spec.
                 (c) Architectural content not in
                     diagrams — amend 0500000
                     diagrams FIRST per DD-002 /
                     DD-003 before retirement.

          S-2  Diagram amendments for (c) gaps under
               DEC-003 Path A one-diagram-per-session
               cadence.

          S-3  Parent spec gap-fill amendments
               (coding-unique content migration).

          S-4  Subordinate spec retirement (git rm +
               commit + push per §11 standing
               practice).

          S-5  Cascade-anchor revision (1010000
               Trading_System_Coding_Anchor for
               AA=10 retirements; 0810000 Trading_
               System_Modules_Anchor for AA=08
               retirements; corresponding AA=04 /
               AA=06 / AA=07 anchors as required).

          S-6  Governance updates (TB00000 + 0311001
               + 0311002 amendments as required by
               the streamlined corpus structure).

        V-038 ENFORCEMENT EXTENSION.
        Per 0311001 v1_15 §15.14.2 SCOPE EXTENSION
        (TB00237 AMENDMENT C companion enactment),
        V-038 diagram-vs-prose authority parity
        validation extends from within-document scope
        (the original v1_10 §15.14 binding) to
        cross-document scope: V-038 validates AA=04 +
        AA=06 + AA=07 + AA=08 + AA=10 subordinate-
        spec content against 0500000 diagram encoding
        at every cross-doc amendment cycle. The
        retirement gate above is enforced by V-038
        before any S-4 git rm action.

        RELATIONSHIP TO DD-001/002/003.
        DD-001 and DD-002 establish the within-
        document authority hierarchy. DD-003
        establishes the 4-step workflow within a
        diagram-bearing document. DD-012 extends the
        same authority hierarchy and workflow ACROSS
        documents in the AA=04/06/07/08/10 corpus,
        with 0500000 as the canonical anchor and the
        subordinate specs as derived restatements
        subject to retirement when the anchor fully
        encodes the element.

        RELATIONSHIP TO DEC-012.
        DEC-012 (TB00153 Decision_Register entry
        ratified at TB00190; campaign-scope extended
        at TB00237 AMENDMENT B from 10XXXXX-only to
        10XXXXX + 08XXXXX + future AA=04/06/07
        candidates) is the operational decision
        directing the execution of the DD-012
        retirement campaign. DD-012 is the absolute-
        standing-rule layer that codifies the
        underlying principle; DEC-012 is the
        campaign-execution decision.

        PRE-EMIT SCAN — DD-012.
        Before authoring any subordinate spec
        amendment in AA=04/06/07/08/10, Claude
        verifies:
          (1) The architectural elements asserted in
              the amendment are encoded in 0500000
              diagrams (V-038 cross-check); OR
          (2) The 0500000 diagram is being amended
              FIRST in the same session under DD-002
              / DD-003 / DEC-003 Path A cadence; OR
          (3) The amendment is coding-unique content
              with no architectural meaning per the
              DEC-012(c) three-bucket classification.

        If none of (1)-(3) applies, the subordinate-
        spec amendment is a DD-012 violation and the
        spec content should instead be authored in
        the 0500000 diagram.

        Self-catch on violation:

          DD-012 self-caught — subordinate-spec
          architecture without 0500000 diagram
          encoding — redrafting.

        RECURRENCE TRACKING.
        Every DD-012 violation is logged in the
        current session's Session Log under "Claude
        Errors This Session" with rule cited (DD-012),
        defect described verbatim, and corrective
        taken. NSI files carry the cumulative
        recurrence count forward. Cumulative DD-012
        violation count at v2_38 enactment = 0.

        CLOSES.
        OI-NEW DD-012-CROSS-DOCUMENT-DIAGRAM-AUTHORITY
        per TB00236 SL §4 + TB00237 NSI §3.1.
        Originating diagnosis: TB00236 chat-turn 2
        Bill verbatim directive "0500000 are canonical
        and authoritative and should replace ALL
        OTHER DOCUMENTS WHERE POSSIBLE." FP/DP
        analysis + Bill ratification: same chat-turn.
        Enacted: TB00237 v2_38.

DD-013  REPO-ROUTING PRE-EMIT SCAN — DD-CLASS
        ABSOLUTE STANDING RULE (NEW v2_48 — TB00315
        AMENDMENT enacting TB00315 NSI v1_1 §3.7
        + §5.11 governance-amendment mission).

        ELEVATION RATIONALE.
        Repository routing for controlled document
        commits is governed by §11 STORAGE +
        §4.1.2 DR-008.6 OPERATION 4 canonical repo
        routing rules (i)/(ii)/(iii). These rules
        have existed in TB00000 since v2_42 (§11
        STORAGE third repo entry + DR-008.6
        OPERATION 4 canonical repo routing
        sub-block) and were refined at v2_44
        (§11 STORAGE TB-PREFIX FILING CONVENTION).
        Cumulative routing-error count at TB00315
        baseline = 4+ (three NSI text occurrences
        across the TB00280 + TB00305 + TB00315
        NSI v1_0 cluster citing TB-prefix files
        as TothBot_V2-Docs/03XXXXX_Governance/
        committed + one OPERATION 4 attempt
        recurrence at TB00314).

        Per TB00000 v2_25 §4.5 DD-010 governance-
        pattern principle — only enforcement-gate
        governance succeeds for behavior-class
        defects in this project (RR-RAT-001
        third-occurrence threshold; OI-037
        six-recurrence historical precedent
        across TB00114-TB00119 under lesson-
        text-only governance; DR-008 three-
        recurrence series TB00169 + TB00170 +
        TB00171 closed by DR-008.9 DD-class
        elevation; RR-SCOPE-005 three-recurrence
        series TB00171 chat-turns 1/2/4 closed
        by DD-011 elevation; FM-001 three-
        recurrence cluster TB00170 + TB00171 +
        TB00172 closed by §4.6 enactment;
        RR-SHELL-008 OPERATION 4 ground-truth
        cluster closed by v2_44 AMENDMENT 2) —
        REPO-ROUTING discipline is hereby
        ELEVATED to DD-class absolute standing
        rule with explicit PRE-EMIT SCAN +
        self-catch enforcement gate matching the
        DD-001..DD-012 + RR-SCOPE-007..010 +
        RR-SHELL-001..008 + PA-001..010 +
        FM-001..007 + DR-008.9 enforcement
        pattern.

        RULE STATEMENT.
        Before emitting any text citing a commit
        destination for any controlled document
        (in NSI body, SL body, OPERATION 4 copy
        box payload, chat-turn prose, or any
        other authoring surface), Claude verifies
        the destination against TB00000 §11
        STORAGE canonical repo routing rules.

        ROUTING RULE (i): TB-PREFIX FILES.
          ALL files whose filename begins with
          the literal token "TB" followed by
          digits (TBNNNNN) MUST route to
          TothBot_V2-SessionLogs/. Includes:
            - TBxxxxx Session Logs (TBxxxxx_
              TothBot_V2_Session_Log_*).
            - TBxxxxx Next Session Instructions
              (TBxxxxx_Next_Session_
              Instructions_*).
            - TB00000 Project Instructions
              (TB00000_TothBot_V2_Project_
              Instructions_*).
            - TB00153 Master_Defect_Register
              (TB00153_Master_Defect_
              Register_*).
            - TB00153 Decision_Register
              (TB00153_Decision_Register_*).
            - TB00153 Diagram_Alter_Add_Remove_
              Plan + Tier_1_Context_Diagram_
              Content_Scope.
            - TBxxxxx Gap Registers (TBxxxxx_
              S1XX_DD012_Phase1_Gap_Register_*).
            - Any other TB-prefix controlled
              document.

        ROUTING RULE (ii): DCN-NUMBERED FILES.
          DCN-numbered files (0XXXXXXX through
          11XXXXX with 7-digit AABCDDD DCN format
          per 0311001 v1_18 §4) MUST route to
          TothBot_V2-Docs/<DCN-folder>/ per
          0311001 v1_18 §7 folder structure
          (00XXXXX through 11XXXXX domain
          folders). Includes governance documents,
          specifications, coding specs, anchors,
          and instance documents.

        ROUTING RULE (iii): CODE FILES.
          Python package code + operations/ +
          tests/ MUST route to TothBot_V2-Code
          per 0311001 v1_18 §3.

        PRE-EMIT SCAN SEQUENCE.
        Before emitting any commit-destination
        citation:
          (1) Enumerate every commit-destination
              citation in the planned response
              (NSI body §X.Y references; SL §X.Y
              references; OPERATION 4 copy box
              cd-target paths; chat-turn prose
              path citations).
          (2) For each citation: extract the
              filename or filename prefix being
              committed.
          (3) Match the filename prefix to
              routing rule (i) / (ii) / (iii)
              per the dispatch logic above.
          (4) Verify the cited destination path
              matches the rule-mandated repo +
              folder.
          (5) If any citation mismatches the
              rule-mandated path: halt response
              emission, redraft with corrected
              path, re-scan before emit.

        SELF-CATCH ON VIOLATION.

          REPO-ROUTING self-caught — [filename]
          routed to [wrong-path] instead of
          [correct-path] — redrafting.

        SCOPE.
        DD-013 applies to ANY text Claude emits
        that cites a commit destination, in any
        authoring surface: NSI body, SL body,
        OPERATION 4 copy box payload, chat-turn
        prose, governance-document amendment
        text, MDR / DR entry path-citation
        fields. The defining characteristic is
        the citation of a commit destination —
        a repository + folder path where a
        controlled document is being or will be
        stored.

        EXCEPTIONS.
        DD-013 does NOT apply when:
          (a) Quoting verbatim from a historical
              session log or NSI where the
              citation was incorrect (forensic
              record preservation per CI-005 +
              CI-006).
          (b) Describing the routing-error
              pattern itself for analysis or
              recurrence-tracking purposes.
          (c) Citing the archive repositories
              (github.com/TothBot/TothBot-Docs
              + github.com/TothBot/TothBot-Code
              read-only archives per §11 STORAGE
              Archive entry).

        RECURRENCE TRACKING.
        Every DD-013 violation is logged in the
        current session's Session Log under
        "Claude Errors This Session" with rule
        cited (DD-013), defect described
        verbatim (filename + wrong path + correct
        path), and corrective taken. NSI files
        carry the cumulative recurrence count
        forward. Cumulative DD-013 violation
        count at v2_48 enactment = 4+ (carry-
        forward from TB00315 baseline pre-
        enactment count per §5.11 of TB00315
        NSI v1_1).

        CROSS-REFERENCES.
        DD-013 instantiates the §11 STORAGE +
        §4.1.2 DR-008.6 OPERATION 4 routing
        rules as an enforcement-gate-level
        rule. The three routing rules
        themselves continue to be defined in

        TB00280 + TB00305 + TB00315 NSI v1_0

        v2_42 §11 STORAGE + §4.1.2 DR-008.6
        OPERATION 4 routing rule (i)) did NOT
        prevent recurrent NSI authoring drift.

        Empirical pattern matches the §4.5
        DD-010 governance-pattern principle:
        behavior-class defects require pre-emit
        scan + self-catch enforcement gates;
        lesson-text-only governance has 100%
        failure rate for behavior-class defects
        in this project (six OI-037 recurrences
        TB00114-TB00119; DR-008 three-recurrence
        cluster; RR-SCOPE-005 three-recurrence
        cluster; FM-001 three-recurrence cluster;
        RR-SHELL-008 OPERATION 4 ground-truth
        cluster). Enforcement-gate governance
