                    Pre-emit scan checks for explicit
                    branch-name token cited in push

                    per (a)/(b)/(c) rule statement.

                    "OVER AND OVER AND OVER AND OVER

                      Long_Module and Short_Module pay

                      module-level. UNIVERSAL annotation

                      detects fee-tier changes from

                      proposes updated values); not a
                      hardcoded floor and not a Bill-
                      controlled wallet-funding
                      parameter.

                    REQUIREMENT in §4.3.3.

                    for any shell command intended for
                    PowerShell execution. Pattern:
                    `cmd /c '...'`. Prohibits double-
                    quote outer wrap which triggers
                    PowerShell variable-expansion +
                    special-character pre-parsing. Pre-

                    ("RR-SHELL-005 self-caught —
                    PowerShell double-quote outer wrap
                    detected — redrafting"). Closes
                    TB00282 SL v1_1 §8.4 recurrent

                    ASCII-ONLY COMMIT-MESSAGE
                    REQUIREMENT in §4.3.3.
                    Mandates ASCII-only commit messages
                    (printable 7-bit ASCII range
                    0x20-0x7E). Prohibits §, →, em-dash,
                    en-dash, smart quotes, ellipsis,
                    parentheses-in-narrative-prose,
                    unbalanced internal quotes,
                    backticks. Standard substitution
                    table provided (§ -> "section ",
                    → -> "->", — -> " - ", etc.). Pre-
                    emit scan + self-catch
                    ("RR-SHELL-006 self-caught — non-
                    ASCII commit message detected —
                    redrafting"). Closes TB00282 SL
                    v1_1 §8.4 commit-message-character-
                    class defect class.

                    AMENDMENT D — RR-SHELL-007
                    SINGLE-COPY-BOX-PER-TURN
                    REQUIREMENT in §4.3.3.
                    Mandates exactly ONE operational
                    shell-command copy box per chat-turn
                    response. Multi-step sequences are
                    delivered one step per turn with
                    Bill confirmation between steps.
                    Permitted exceptions: commands
                    joined by && or ; (atomic
                    operation); single-logical-action
                    sequences (cd + git add/commit/push
                    for one push); explicit Bill
                    request for multi-step delivery in

                          Problem NOT gone — percentile
                          computation still requires a

                          load-bearing.

                          preserved? Yes — by absorbing
                          into §9.17 registry.

                      registry entry — atr_rolling_window

                      be absorbed BEFORE retirement

                      gap between absorption and
                      retirement). Same-session

  v2_32 2026-05-12  §11 STORAGE AMENDMENT — RETIRED-
                    DOCUMENT STANDING-PRACTICE CODIFICATION
                    (TB00223 ENACTMENT PER BILL CHAT-TURN
                    DIRECTIVE).

                    One new subsection added to §11
                    STORAGE between the VPS subsection and
                    the existing "Archive (read-only —
                    reference only)" subsection. The new
                    "Retired documents (TothBot_V2-Docs
                    and TothBot_V2-Code)" subsection
                    codifies Bill standing practice for
                    retired controlled documents:

                      (a) Retirement = `git rm` + commit +
                          push (single commit, single
                          operation; no rename, no
                          successor file).
                      (b) Git history preserves all prior
                          versions of the document. Use
                          `git log --follow <path>` to
                          inspect full version history.
                      (c) No _Archive folder anywhere
                          (local, remote, or VPS).
                      (d) No rt-prefix successor file
                          (rt1_0, rt1_3, etc.) authored
                          or committed at HEAD.
                      (e) No tombstone-document body
                          (the 1011005 rt1_3 pattern at
                          TB00220 was the originating
                          mistake; see TB00220 SL §4.1
                          forensic record).
                      (f) Retirement removes the file
                          from the Claude.ai project
                          knowledge folder, the local C:
                          working tree, AND GitHub HEAD;
                          the document continues to exist
                          as history in git only.

                    The new subsection contains an
                    explicit supersession clause: any
                    prior text in this document, in
                    0311003 Versioning_Procedure VP-010(c),
                    in 0311001 §8.7 folder structure, or
                    in any prior session log or NSI that
                    prescribes a local _Archive folder, an
                    rt-prefix file at HEAD, or a tombstone
                    document body is SUPERSEDED by this
                    standing practice.

                    Governance amendments to 0311003 +
                    0311001 to reconcile their text with
                    this practice are carry-forwards
                    (TB00224 NSI).

                    REASON FOR CHANGE.
                    Bill TB00223 chat-turn explicit
                    directive following Phase 3
                    governance-conflict surface in this
                    session's 1011008 Long_Module
                    retirement cascade. The TB00223 NSI
                    §3.5 prescribed the rt-rename
                    methodology with "insert retirement
                    marker per 0311003 retirement-marker
                    template" — a Claude-fabricated
                    procedural directive that does not
                    appear in 0311003. Bill chat-turn
                    clarifications in sequence:

                      (1) "retirement means the old file
                          DISAPPEARS" — meaning removed
                          from Claude, retired on
                          GitHub, no longer used.
                      (2) "A rt-state file is moved to
                          GitHub. That is the only place
                          a rt-state file lives. It will
                          be removed from C: and Claude
                          Project Folder." — clarified
                          that rt-state means lives in
                          GitHub only, removed from
                          local working tree and project
                          folder.
                      (3) "The document with all of it's
                          revisions and histories lives
                          on GitHub. It is my
                          understanding that is what
                          GitHub is for. It stores every
                          version so there is a version
                          history." — final clarification
                          that GIT HISTORY is the
                          version archive; the file at
                          HEAD does not need a rt-prefix
                          rename or a tombstone body.
                          The plain `git rm` + commit +
                          push captures the retirement
                          state-change; `git log`
                          retrieves the version history.

  v2_29 2026-05-10  PARALLEL-MODULE FRAMEWORK + PER-MODULE
                    WALLETS + SACRED-FLOOR R:R + R:R-DRIVEN
                    SIZING CURVE + PER-MODULE CIATS —
                    TB00179 STAGE M-2 PARAMETER FOUNDATION.

                    Major rewrite of §9 Trading System Rules.
                    Substantive content changes across §9.1
                    through §9.10, §9.16 amendment, and full
                    §9.17 CIATS Parameter Registry rewrite.
                    No changes outside §9 and §12.

                    SCOPE OF CHANGES:

                    (1) §9.3 — PARALLEL-MODULE FRAMEWORK
                        NEW. Codifies parallel, independent
                        trading modules (Long_Module,
                        Short_Module, future modules) as
                        siblings with own universe scope,
                        own gate thresholds, own wallets,
                        own sizing function, own CIATS
                        instance, own drawdown halts.
                        Shared WS Manager at data-
                        acquisition layer only (Kraken WS
                        rate-limit constraint per
                        empirical TB00141/TB00142
                        validation). Every layer above
                        WS Manager is module-independent.

                    (2) §9.4 — OPERATOR-CONTROLLED WALLET
                        FUNDING NEW. Each module's
                        trading wallet is funded by Bill
                        with affordable-loss capital.
                        Wallet funding is the primary loss
                        control. CIATS does not own wallet
                        balances. Paper-trading starting
                        balances: $5,000 per module
                        (Long + Short). Live wallet
                        amounts are a separate Bill
                        decision informed by paper-trading
                        results.

                    (3) §9.6 — PER-MODULE CIATS FRAMEWORK
                        NEW. Each module gets its own
                        CIATS instance with its own
                        statistical pool, own 200-trade
                        inference threshold, own 600-trade
                        per-regime threshold, own
                        parameter proposals. Cross-module
                        data contamination prohibited.

                    (4) §9.7 — PER-WALLET DRAWDOWN HALTS
                        NEW. Drawdown thresholds evaluated
                        per-module-wallet, not per-
                        portfolio. Long drawdown halt
                        does not halt Short, and vice
                        versa. Both thresholds CIATS-
                        owned starting values (5% session-
                        pause, 10% full-halt per-wallet).

                    (5) §9.10 — SACRED CONSTRAINT REWRITE.
                        Net 1:1.5 R:R is the MINIMUM
                        expected R:R on every trade (not
                        a fixed ratio). CIATS owns the
                        sizing curve ABOVE the floor.
                        Trades with expected R:R above
                        1:1.5 may receive larger
                        allocations. Per-trade sizing is
                        a CIATS-owned function of
                        expected R:R, bounded above by
                        per_trade_ceiling_pct (25%
                        starting). Acceptance rule A1:
                        reject at point-estimate below
                        1:1.5. CIATS may NEVER propose
                        below-floor trades; CIATS MAY
                        propose larger allocations and
                        adjust the sizing curve form.

                    (6) §9.16 — PARAMETER PHILOSOPHY
                        AMENDED. Adds per-module
                        instantiation clarification.
                        Updates sacred-value reference
                        from generic "net 1:1.5 R:R" to
                        explicit "§9.10 net 1:1.5 R:R
                        minimum floor."

                    (7) §9.17 — CIATS PARAMETER REGISTRY
                        FULL REWRITE. New classification
                        scheme (SACRED / OPERATOR / CIATS-
                        OWNED / RETIRED). Per-module
                        instantiation. R:R-driven sizing.
                        Short-side parameters added
                        (leverage_cap_short = 3x,
                        rsi_short_low = 70, rsi_short_high
                        = 50, min_order_size_usd = Kraken
                        per-pair minimum). Retired:
                        tradeable_pct, per_trade_pct,
                        max_concurrent, Half-Kelly
                        transition rule.

                    (8) §9.5 — NOTIFICATIONS section
                        renumbered from prior §9.7
                        (alerts@tothbot.com routing
                        unchanged).

                    (9) §9.8, §9.9 — Exit Controller and
                        Kraken resting SL sections
                        renumbered but content unchanged.

                    RETIRED §9 RULES (with verbatim pre-
                    amendment text preserved per CI-005 +
                    CI-006):
                      §9.3 (v2_28): "Tradeable capital =
                        Portfolio x 0.50 (starting)"
                      §9.4 (v2_28): "Single trade size =
                        tradeable x 0.05 (starting).
                        Transitions to Half-Kelly at 200
                        closed trades."
                      §9.5 (v2_28): "Max 20 concurrent
                        positions (starting)."
                      §9.6 (v2_28): "Long Module only.
                        Short Module deferred."
                      §9.10 (v2_28): "Net 1:1.5 R:R is
                        the only hardcoded constraint.
                        CIATS does not own this. It is
                        sacred."

                    RETIRED §9.17 (v2_28) — full pre-

                    REASON FOR CHANGE:
                    Stage M-2 (short-side parameter
                    starting values + 0811005 Short_Module
                    Specification authoring per DEC-011
                    Option C sequencing) requires the
                    parameter foundation in TB00000 to
                    reflect short-side architecture before
                    downstream specifications can be
                    authored consistently. Bill chat-turn
                    sequence at TB00179 (chat-turns 2-7)
                    ratified the parallel-module
                    framework, per-module CIATS, per-
                    wallet drawdowns, sacred-floor R:R,
                    R:R-driven sizing curve with A1
                    acceptance rule and B2 per-trade
                    ceiling, $5,000-per-module paper
                    wallet starting balances, and Kraken-
                    minimum per_trade_size_usd starting
                    value (CIATS-owned from paper-trading
                    data threshold forward).

                    FP/DP ANALYSIS — PER-MODULE CIATS
                    OPTION B vs SINGLE-CIATS-WITH-SHORT-
                    HOOKS OPTION A.
                    Option A (shared CIATS with branching
                      logic for direction) — REJECTED.
                      Less work in M-5 but contaminates
                      module statistical pools and
                      bottlenecks future-module additions.
                    Option B (per-module CIATS instance)
                      — ACCEPTED. Matches parallel-module
                      framework. Trivial to add modules.
                      Long and Short statistical pools
                      stay independent. Loss-prevention
                      mission better served by per-
                      module statistical confidence than
                      mixed-pool contamination.

                    FP/DP ANALYSIS — A1 vs A2 EXPECTED-
                    R:R ACCEPTANCE RULE.
                    Option A1 (reject at point-estimate)
                      — ACCEPTED. Maximum trade count
                      for CIATS data accumulation during
                      paper trading. Aligns with
                      maximum-CIATS-latitude principle.
                    Option A2 (reject at confidence-
                      bounded estimate) — REJECTED for
                      paper-trading start. Stricter
                      but reduces trade count during
                      the most data-hungry phase. CIATS
                      may propose A2 once empirical
                      false-acceptance-rate data
                      justifies.

                    FP/DP ANALYSIS — B2 PER-TRADE
                    CEILING vs B1 NO-CEILING vs B3
                    SACRED-CEILING.
                    Option B1 (no ceiling) — REJECTED.
                      A wrong R:R estimate at high
                      allocation could wipe an entire
                      wallet in one trade.
                    Option B2 (25% wallet starting,
                      CIATS-adjustable) — ACCEPTED.
                      Keeps sizing curve CIATS-owned
                      above the floor. Prevents early-
                      paper-trading single-trade
                      wipeout. CIATS adjusts on
                      evidence.
                    Option B3 (sacred ceiling) —
                      REJECTED. Conflicts with maximum-
                      CIATS-latitude principle.

                    FP/DP ANALYSIS — $5,000 PER-MODULE
                    PAPER WALLET.
                    Three constraints govern:
                    (1) Slot count must allow gates to
                        be exercised — $5,000 wallet ÷
                        $0.50 minimum trade = 10,000
                        theoretical slots; well above
                        any realistic concurrent count.
                    (2) Drawdown halts must not fire
                        from normal variance —
                        5%/$250 and 10%/$500 thresholds
                        on $5,000 wallet are in the
                        "halts trigger occasionally"
                        zone CIATS needs.
                    (3) Time to 200 trades (CIATS
                        Proposal Engine activation
                        per §7) must be reasonable —
                        wallet capacity is not the
                        bottleneck at $5,000 scale.

                    Smaller wallets (e.g. $500) cap the
                    high-R:R sizing curve before CIATS
                    can differentiate trade qualities
                    and trigger halts too frequently.
                    Larger wallets (e.g. $50,000) make
                    halts effectively never fire,
                    suppressing the drawdown-event data
                    class CIATS needs.

                    SUPERSESSION:
                    §9.10 (v2_28) statement "Net 1:1.5
                    R:R is the only hardcoded constraint.
                    CIATS does not own this. It is
                    sacred." is replaced by the §9.10
                    (v2_29) statement that makes 1:1.5
                    a MINIMUM FLOOR rather than a fixed
                    ratio. CIATS may invest more on
                    higher-expected-R:R trades. CIATS
                    may never accept, size, or propose
                    below-floor trades. The interpretive
                    shift is from "1:1.5 = the R:R" to
                    "1:1.5 = the floor; CIATS owns
                    everything above."

                    Legacy D-05 paper_starting_balance =
                    $1,000 single-pool value is
                    SUPERSEDED by paper_starting_balance_
                    long_usd = $5,000 + paper_starting_
                    balance_short_usd = $5,000 (per-
                    module). D-05 itself updated in a
                    later Stage M-2 spec-content session
                    (M-1 carry-forward per TB00175 SL
                    §3.1.2).

  v2_9  2026-04-18  Section 11 Storage updated.
                    Session logs and TB00000 location changed
                    to co-locate with the two git repos under
                    the TothBot parent folder:
                      C:\Users\wstot\GitHub\TothBot\
                        TBXXXXX_Session_Logs\

                    REASON FOR CHANGE:
                    Platform transition from Claude Chat to
                    Claude Code. Claude Chat could access the
                    Claude.ai project folder directly, so the
                    physical location of session logs on disk
                    was decoupled from Claude's access path.
                    Claude Code does NOT have access to the
                    Claude.ai project folder. Claude Code
                    operates exclusively on a single file-
                    system tree rooted at its launch
                    directory.

                    FP/DP ANALYSIS:
                    Option A (keep prior path) would require
                    launching Claude Code from C:\Users\wstot\
                    to reach both the GitHub folder and the
                    session logs location. This exposes the
                    entire user profile (.ssh keys, Documents,
                    Downloads, AppData, Desktop, browser
                    profiles) to Claude Code. Violation of
                    least-privilege. Larger scan tree slows
                    every tool call. Multiple possible
                    launch directories increase error rate.

                    Option B (co-locate in TothBot) limits
                    Claude Code scope to TothBot content
                    only. Three subfolders: two git repos
                    plus session logs. Least-privilege
                    preserved. Faster tool calls. Single
                    canonical launch directory:
                      C:\Users\wstot\GitHub\TothBot\

                    Decision: Option B. Efficiency,
                    reliability, and safety all improve.
                    The only cost is this one-time document
                    update to ratify the new location.

                    TB00000's own DocPath updated to the
                    new location (TB00000 lives alongside
                    the session logs).
                    Document Status updated: supersedes v2_8.

  v2_10 2026-04-20  Section 9.7 updated. Notification routing

                    "550 5.1.1 Recipient address rejected".
                    Bill detected the live defects
                    (WS_MGR_FATAL, Kraken EAPI:Invalid key

                    the CRITICAL events themselves were
                    invisible because their alerts never
                    reached the inbox.

                    Option A (create singular mailbox in
                    Proton) rejected — Proton catch-all
                    blocks creation; external dependency.
                    Option B (rename plural mailbox to
                    singular) rejected — would invert the
                    problem and invalidate every existing
                    reference (git history, spec docs,
                    alert archive). Option C (change code

  v2_14 2026-04-25  OI-054-CAND CLOSURE — DR-002 GOVERNANCE
                    REFINEMENT.

                    Two new rules added to Section 4.1:
                    DR-004 BINARY ARTIFACT INTEGRITY
                    VALIDATION (mandatory file-type and
                    structural probes for every binary
                    artifact, plus the .docx settings.xml
                    validate.py gate established in
                    TB00130) and DR-005 CANONICAL NAMING
                    OF THREE-FORMAT COMPONENTS (canonical
                    filename patterns and version-triplet
                    consistency rule for 0500000 .txt /
                    .docx / .pdf set).

                    REASON FOR CHANGE:
                    Two governance gaps surfaced in
                    TB00130 (ERROR-TB00130-01 .docx
                    settings.xml validation defect) and
                    TB00134 (ERROR-PRE-001 plain-text-
                    mislabeled-as-.docx defect, plus
                    missing .pdf for 0500000 dv1_20).
                    Both are documented as OI-054-CAND
                    DR-002-DOCX-REQUIREMENT-UNACHIEVABLE-
                    THROUGH-PLATFORM and have been
                    blocking 0500000 three-format
                    delivery confidence across multiple
                    sessions.

                    DR-004 codifies the required pre-
                    delivery integrity checks. Every
                    binary artifact passes BOTH a `file`
                    type probe AND a container structural
                    probe before present_files is called.
                    .docx additionally passes the
                    validate.py settings.xml gate.
                    Failure handling is explicit: do not
                    deliver, log as Claude error per
                    RR-VIOL-002.

                    DR-005 codifies canonical naming so
                    Bill's project folder cannot end up
                    with mixed-version triplets or
                    suffix confusion. Pre-flight STEP A
                    in NSIs must verify version-triplet
                    consistency.

                    FP/DP ANALYSIS:
                    Option A (rely on existing DR-002
                    text alone) — REJECTED. DR-002
                    establishes the three-format
                    requirement but does not specify
                    integrity checks. Two consecutive
                    sessions (TB00130 / TB00134) produced
                    integrity-failed deliveries. DR-002
                    text alone is insufficient.
                    Option B (retire .docx delivery and
                    keep .txt + .pdf only) — REJECTED.
                    Bill's downstream Word workflow
                    requires .docx. Retiring shifts the
                    burden to Bill (manual export). Net
                    cost higher than fixing the integrity
                    gates.

  v2_23 2026-05-09  DIAGRAMS AS CANONICAL DESIGN
                    DOCUMENTS — NEW SECTION 4.5
                    ABSOLUTE STANDING RULE.

                    One new section added to §4.4 ->
                    §4.5 transition: §4.5 DIAGRAMS
                    AS CANONICAL DESIGN DOCUMENTS as
                    ABSOLUTE STANDING RULE. Ten
                    rules (DD-001 through DD-010)
                    codify the architectural
                    principle that diagrams in
                    0500000 (and future Tier-2-and-
                    below diagram-bearing controlled
                    documents) are the authoritative
                    source for all architectural
                    rules, contracts, decisions,
                    gates, layers, regimes,
                    parameters, containers, modules,
                    indicators, events, channels,
                    architectural reasoning entries,
                    and pt_mode identifiers they
                    encode. Prose contextualizes;
                    prose does NOT govern. When
                    prose and diagram conflict, the
                    diagram governs.

                    Section structure:
                      DD-001  Diagrams are the
                              canonical design
                              documents.
                      DD-002  Diagram-over-prose
                              authority hierarchy.
                      DD-003  The 4-step workflow
                              (diagrams -> prose ->
                              10XXXXX -> code).
                      DD-004  No prose-first
                              authoring.
                      DD-005  Conflict-detection
                              validation (V-038
                              cross-check).
                      DD-006  Recurrence tracking.
                      DD-007  Pre-emit scan +
                              self-catch ("DD
                              self-caught — prose-
                              first authoring
                              detected — redrafting").
                      DD-008  Rationale (TB00152
                              SL §5.1 verbatim
                              quote + TB00163
                              chat-turn 4
                              reaffirmation +
                              first-principles
                              O(N²) -> O(N) drift-
                              detection analysis).
                      DD-009  Relationship to
                              0311001 §15.13 HTML
                              canonical format
                              (complementary, not
                              redundant).
                      DD-010  Supersession of
                              prior lesson-text.

                    REASON FOR CHANGE:
                    TB00163 SL v1_1 §7.4 surfaced
                    the DIAGRAMS-AS-CANONICAL
                    governance gap as CRITICAL
                    after the diagrams-completed
                    verification challenge. Bill's
                    chat-turn directive: "Provide

                    This is the only priority
                    until it is completed."

  v2_22 2026-05-08  DR-008 VERY SHORT CHAT START COPY BOX
                    — NEW DELIVERY RULE.

                    One new rule added to Section 4.1.2:
                    DR-008 VERY SHORT CHAT START COPY BOX.
                    Pre-emit-scan + self-catch governance
                    pattern matching the §4.1 DR-004
                    through DR-007 / §4.2 / §4.3 / §4.4
                    enforcement structure. Mandates that
                    every session-close turn that produces
                    a Next Session Instructions (NSI)
                    document MUST also produce a
                    copy-box-ready VERY SHORT chat-start
                    string for the receiving session.

                    Section 4.1.2 heading updated: "(DR-001
                    THROUGH DR-007)" -> "(DR-001 THROUGH
                    DR-008)".

                    Section 4.1.6 self-catch-signal scope
                    extended: "DR-004 through DR-007" ->
                    "DR-004 through DR-008". DR-008
                    self-catch signal pattern added:
                      "DR-008 self-caught — chat start
                       missing — redrafting."

                    REASON FOR CHANGE:
                    Bill standing operational practice
                    requires every session start to have a
                    copy-box-ready trigger string. Prior
                    sessions delivered NSIs without bundled
                    chat-start strings, forcing Bill to
                    author the chat-start string manually
                    each session. Manual chat-start
                    authoring is recurrence-prone (wrong
                    filename, wrong Stage, missing
                    deliverable). The bundling needs to
                    happen at the same enforcement-gate
                    layer that produces the NSI itself, so
                    a session cannot ship an NSI without
                    the chat-start string.

                    FP/DP ANALYSIS:
                    Option A (codify DR-008 as absolute
                    standing rule with pre-emit scan +
                    self-catch + recurrence tracking) —
                    ACCEPTED. Matches the only governance
                    pattern with 100% success rate for
                    behavior-class defects in this project
                    (§4.1 DR-007 + §4.2 OneDrive ban + §4.3
                    RR-SCOPE-007/008/009/010 + §4.4
                    PA-001..010 — zero recurrences
                    post-enactment).
                    Option B (lesson-text recommendation,
                    "include a chat-start copy box where
                    helpful") — REJECTED. Identical defect
                    class to lesson-text-only governance
                    which failed six consecutive times for
                    OI-037. Format guidance without
                    enforcement gates does not work in
                    this project.
                    Option C (separate Bill chat-message
                    template that Bill maintains externally
                    to project) — REJECTED. Same recurrence
                    exposure as today; defeats the purpose
                    of project-internal governance.

                    Decision: Option A.

                    PROCEDURAL NOTE — DIRECTIVE ORIGIN.
                    Bill chat-turn directive in TB00157
                    Stage D execution session: "amend
                    TB00000 Project Instructions §4.1 to
                    add a 'VERY SHORT Chat Start' delivery
                    rule." Amendment authored same turn
                    as Stage D D7 R1 -> R2 rework batch
                    delivery, per single-turn delivery
                    contract (DR-006).

  v2_21 2026-05-08  RR-SCOPE-010 NSI IDENTIFIER-CITATION
                    DISCIPLINE — NEW STANDING RULE.

                    One new rule added to Section 4.3.1:
                    RR-SCOPE-010 NSI IDENTIFIER-CITATION
                    DISCIPLINE. Pre-emit-scan + self-catch
                    governance pattern matching the §4.2 /
                    §4.3 RR-SCOPE-007/008/009 / §4.4
                    enforcement structure. Mandates that
                    every rule:/contract:/ar:/decision:/
                    gate:/layer:/regime:/pt_mode:/param:/
                    container:/mod:/indicator:/evt:/
                    channel: identifier cited in any Next
                    Session Instructions document MUST be
                    grep-verified against the current
                    authoritative spec at the moment of
                    NSI authoring.

                    Section 4.3 lead-in updated:
                    RR-SCOPE-001 through RR-SCOPE-009 ->
                    RR-SCOPE-001 through RR-SCOPE-010.
                    OI closure list extended to include
                    OI-085.

                    REASON FOR CHANGE:
                    TB00155 SL §7 surfaced an HR-WM-032
                    vs WM-PACE-002 spec-discrepancy in
                    the prior session's NSI (TB00155 NSI
                    v1_0). TB00155 NSI cited "HR-WM-032
                    SUBSCRIBE_RATE_PER_SEC = 10" as the
                    token-bucket rule. Per current spec
                    (0511001 dv1_5), HR-WM-032 is
                    "PAPER LEDGER UPDATE" — a different
                    rule entirely. The token bucket is
                    governed by contract:WM-PACE-002 in
                    1011002 dv1_26 §4.7. The NSI cited
                    the wrong identifier from quick
                    reference / paraphrase rather than
                    grep-verification against the current
                    spec.

                    TB00155 caught the error during
                    cold-load by reading the current spec
                    directly and used the correct
                    identifier in the D1 R2 diagram. The
                    error stayed in the instruction
                    document; it did not propagate to the
                    artifact. But the failure mode is
                    real: a future session that trusts
                    an NSI identifier without spec-
                    grounding could reproduce the wrong
                    reference into a controlled artifact
                    (diagram, code, spec). The governance
                    gap is identical in class to AR-070
                    silent-narrowing (governance-class
                    defect not catchable by lesson text
                    alone).

                    FP/DP ANALYSIS:
                    Option A (codify RR-SCOPE-010 as
                    absolute standing rule with pre-emit
                    scan + self-catch + recurrence
                    tracking) — ACCEPTED. Matches the
                    only governance pattern with 100%
                    success rate for behavior-class
                    defects in this project (§4.2
                    OneDrive ban + §4.3 RR-SCOPE-007/
                    008/009 + §4.4 PA-001..010 — zero
                    recurrences post-enactment).
                    Option B (citation-form
                    recommendation, "cf. spec doc"
                    instead of inline assertion) —
                    REJECTED. Identical defect class to
                    lesson-text-only governance which
                    failed six consecutive times for
                    OI-037. Format guidance without
                    enforcement gates does not work in
                    this project.
                    Option C (structural change — NSIs
                    cease citing identifiers altogether)
                    — REJECTED. No enforcement
                    mechanism (identifiers could still
                    slip through inline by mistake);
                    NSIs become harder to use (more
                    lookup work for the receiving
                    session, less standalone information
                    for Bill).

                    Decision: Option A.

  v2_18 2026-05-03  PAPER-AS-MASTER PRINCIPLE
                    (NEW SECTION 4.4).

                    One new section added to §4.3 -> §4.4
                    transition: §4.4 PAPER-AS-MASTER
                    PRINCIPLE as ABSOLUTE STANDING RULE.
                    Ten rules (PA-001 through PA-010)
                    codify the architectural principle
                    that paper trading is the master
                    configuration and live trading is
                    built to MIMIC paper. Outside the
                    four enumerated PA-004 divergence
                    points, paper and live are byte-
                    identical.

                    Section structure:
                      PA-001  Paper is the master.
                              Live mimics paper.
                      PA-002  ONE set of documents.
                      PA-003  ONE set of code.
                      PA-004  PERMITTED DIVERGENCE
                              POINTS — exactly four
                              (private WS connection;
                              order dispatch; capital
                              ledger; Position Mirror
                              sourcing).
                      PA-005  Everything else byte-
                              identical.
                      PA-006  New divergence points
                              require Bill written
                              authorization.
                      PA-007  Paper canonical for
                              parameter values.
                      PA-008  Pre-emit scan + self-catch
                              ("PA-MASTER self-caught —
                              redrafting").
                      PA-009  Recurrence tracking.
                              Initial cumulative count
                              = 1 (ERROR-TB00145-CHAT-02).
                              OI-073 tracks future
                              recurrence.
                      PA-010  Rationale.

                    REASON FOR CHANGE:
                    ERROR-TB00145-CHAT-02 (PAPER-AS-
                    MASTER VIOLATION). In TB00145 v1_0,
                    Claude authored four primary specs
                    (0511001 dv1_5, 1011002 dv1_26,
                    0211005 dv1_2, 1011014 dv1_8) under
                    a wrong-direction premise: live as
                    canonical with paper as the variant.
                    Bill's standing intent — confirmed
                    explicitly mid-session — is the
                    REVERSE: paper is canonical (because
                    all Kraken WS message-limit testing
                    was done in paper mode), and live
                    must be built to mimic paper.

                    Bill removed all four wrong-direction
                    documents from the project knowledge
                    folder and from local storage.
                    Bill restored the four paper-canonical
                    predecessors (dv1_4, dv1_25, dv1_1,
                    dv1_7) from recycling bin. Bill
                    directed Claude to redo TB00145 SL
                    + NSI as v1_1 and to add a new
                    section to TB00000 codifying the
                    paper-as-master principle.

                    The new §4.4 makes the direction
                    of mimicry unambiguous. PA-004
                    enumerates EXACTLY where paper
                    and live MUST differ — only at the
                    four physical-impossibility
                    boundaries. PA-005 mandates byte-
                    identical behavior everywhere else.
                    PA-006 prohibits new divergence
                    points without Bill written
                    authorization. PA-008 adds the
                    pre-emit scan + self-catch matching
                    the §4.2 / §4.3 enforcement pattern.

                    Option A (carry as NSI lesson text
                      only) REJECTED — NSI lesson text

                    Section 4.3 lead-in updated:
                    RR-SCOPE-001 through RR-SCOPE-008
                    -> RR-SCOPE-001 through
                    RR-SCOPE-009. OI closure list
                    extended to include OI-061.

                    REASON FOR CHANGE:
                    OI-061 D-08_INCOMPLETE_FPDP_
                    CHESTERTONS_FENCE. The D-08 Top-N
                    cap retirement FP/DP analysis did
                    not investigate the cap's origin
                    before recommending removal. The
                    cap was originally a load-bearing
                    constraint preventing universe
                    expansion past the single-
                    connection WS rate-limit
                    ceiling. Removing it without
                    investigating its purpose was
                    the second-order cause of OI-060
                    WS_SUBSCRIBE_RATE_LIMIT_STORM:
                    once Top-N retired, universe
                    grew to 748, single-connection
                    architecture failed, dv1_22
                    deployed without architectural
                    fix, bot crashed. RR-SCOPE-009
                    is the governance fix that
                    would have surfaced the load-
                    bearing nature of D-08 before
                    its retirement.

                    FP/DP ANALYSIS:
                    Option A (carry as NSI lesson
                    text only) -- REJECTED. NSI
                    text governance has demonstrably
                    failed across this project for
                    behavior-class defects.
                    RR-SCOPE-009 is behavior-class
                    (every-response pre-emit scan).
                    Option B (rule with pre-commit
                    gate) -- REJECTED. Pre-commit
                    blocking creates author-friction
                    for review cycles in
                    TothBot_V2-Docs without adding
                    safety. The defect surfaces at
                    deploy, not at commit.
                    Option C (rule with pre-deploy
                    gate, Bill override clause,
                    self-catch signal matching §4.2
                    / §4.3 pattern) -- ACCEPTED.
                    Matches the enforcement pattern
                    that has demonstrably worked in
                    this project. Aligns with
                    DC-PREFLIGHT-006 placement in
                    0311002 v1_8 (companion increment
                    same session).

                    Decision: Option C.

  v2_16 2026-04-25  OI-058 CLOSURE + ERROR-TB00131-01
                    GOVERNANCE — DR-006 DELIVERY-TURN
                    SELF-CONTAINMENT.

                    One new rule added to Section 4.1:
                    DR-006 DELIVERY-TURN SELF-
                    CONTAINMENT (mandatory single-turn
                    rule binding announce + delivery
                    into a single response, with
                    pre-emit scan, self-catch signal,
                    and violation handling). Five
                    sub-rules: DR-006.1 single-turn
                    rule, DR-006.2 pre-emit scan,
                    DR-006.3 self-catch behavior,
                    DR-006.4 scope (applies to all
                    file deliverables including
                    batches), DR-006.5 violation
                    handling.

                    REASON FOR CHANGE:
                    ERROR-TB00131-01 (DELIVERY-
                    SEQUENCING-MISS) originated in
                    TB00131 §12 and surfaced in
                    TB00139 STREAM 3 extraction sweep
                    as Finding 4. The defect: in a
                    spec-delivery turn, Claude
                    announced "Presenting both at
                    Gate 1" but did not call
                    present_files in the same turn.
                    Bill had to send a "Continue"
                    prompt to trigger actual file
                    delivery. NSI text identified the
                    pattern but governance never
                    formalized the rule. Defect class:
                    delivery-turn structure, not shell
                    mechanics.

                    FP/DP ANALYSIS:
                    Option A (DR-006 in §4.1
                    Document Delivery Rules) —
                    semantically aligned: §4.1 houses
                    DR-001 (format), DR-002 (three-
                    format), DR-003 (one-batch),
                    DR-004 (integrity), DR-005
                    (naming). All §4.1 rules concern
                    file-delivery mechanics.
                    DR-006 (single-turn delivery)
                    extends the same family.
                    Option B (RR-SHELL-005 in §4.3.3
                    Shell-Context Completeness) —
                    semantic mismatch: §4.3.3 RR-SHELL
                    rules concern shell command
                    self-containment (cd+command in
                    same copy box, shell wrapper, env
                    vars). ERROR-TB00131-01 is about
                    file delivery turn structure, not
                    shell mechanics. Forcing a shell
                    rule onto a delivery defect
                    creates rule-class drift.

                    Decision: Option A (DR-006).
                    Semantic fit governs. ACCEPTED.

                    PARENT CHAIN COMPLIANCE: TB00000
                    is a controlled document outside
                    the TothBot V2 DCN namespace per
                    Section 1 Document Status. No DCN
                    chain dependencies. Section 12
                    Revision History updated.
